Hangzhou Chamber of Commerce Established

Executive and Supervisory Committee Members Sworn In

Today (the 8th) at around 9:00 AM, the Hangzhou Chamber of Commerce held a swearing-in ceremony for the newly elected fifteen executive committee members, seven alternate executive committee members, seven supervisory committee members, and three alternate supervisors. The attendees included executive committee members Wang Ziqiu, Chen Xingwu, Wang Xiangquan, Xu Xinggong, Wang Zhuzhai, Jin Runquan, Xu Zhen, Cheng Xinjin, Wang Wuquan, Yu Shaoyan, Mi Tingfang, Yang Chunlai, Li Chunzhi, Yao Yinsheng, and Zhang Xuren, alternate executive committee members Xu Da, Qiu Wenyuan, and Yao Runqing, supervisory committee members Xie Hucheng, Cai Liangyou, Wu Jinqing, Ge Anfu, and Yang Yaowen, and alternate supervisors Han Zhixue and Zhou Xiangyai. After the entire group took their oaths, the first executive committee meeting was held to elect standing committee members. The results were: Wang Zhuzhai received fourteen votes, Jin Runquan fourteen votes, Wang Xiangquan thirteen votes, Xu Xinggong thirteen votes, and Mi Tingfang twelve votes, and they were elected as standing committee members. Next, the chairman was elected, and Wang Zhuzhai received thirteen votes and was elected as chairman. The meeting then discussed proposals and adjourned.

Local Correspondence

Suzhou

Further Report on the Arrest of Suspected Reactionaries On the anniversary of the September 18th Incident the other day, Suzhou's defense was very tight. At the entrance to Cu Fang Bridge on Guanqian Street and at the entrance to Jia Lane, a youth carrying reactionary propaganda was arrested, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. When Officer Wang asked his name, the youth said he was Song Qin, 19 years old, from Beigui Town, Jiangyin. He claimed that a Mr. Lu in room 15 of the Continental Hotel had asked him to take the printed materials to Qimen. Officer Wang suspected Song of being a reactionary and took him into custody. He then went to room 15 of the Continental Hotel to see if there was a Mr. Lu. He found people gambling inside and arrested the gamblers Lu Fusheng, Lu Achun, Li Genfa, Wang Jinlin, Yuan Genji, and others. He asked Lu Fusheng and Lu Achun if they knew Song Qin, but they all stared blankly and said they did not. They were taken into custody because they were related to the suspicion. Also, at around 7:00 PM, police officers from the Second Precinct arrested a suspected counter-revolutionary monk in the Sanyuanfang Jiecao Hermitage and took him to the bureau for investigation.

Town Head Carrying a Handgun Li Enchang, the town head of Zhongsi Port in Pingwang District, Wujiang County, came to Suzhou on the 4th of this month with Liu Changgui, a patrol officer from the 8th Sub-bureau of the Pingwang Public Security Bureau, carrying three handguns and twenty-two bullets. They were staying in room 22 of the Central Hotel. The night before, Officer Wang Xunxiang from the 4th Section of the Second Precinct, accompanied by senior police officers, checked the room. When they opened Li's suitcase in room 22, they found three handguns. They asked if he had a permit, and Li said he did not. Officer Wang suspected him and took him and the handguns to the precinct. Yesterday, Section Chief Zhang of the Judicial Section questioned him briefly. The three handguns were kept at the bureau, and after an investigation with the Wujiang County Government, they would be returned. Li Sichang and Liu Changgui were temporarily released on bail pending further summons.

Counter-Revolutionary Criminals from Nantong Escorted to Suzhou The Nantong County Court yesterday (the 8th) dispatched bailiffs Wang Ziqing to escort counter-revolutionary criminals Song Buzhang, Ji Guangsheng, Ding Pengfei, and Zhu Jinkui from Nantong to Suzhou. They were handed over to the Higher Court. After investigation by the prosecutor, they were sent to the prison of this court.

Unexpected Guests Attempted to Borrow Money by Force Jiang Ruojia, the head of the Danyang fellow-villagers association, residing at No. 11 Yiduo Lane in the city, was suddenly visited by two unexpected guests the night before (the 7th) at around 8:00 PM. They attempted to forcibly borrow money from Jiang. Jiang immediately reported this to the 4th Section of the Second Precinct by telephone. Officer Wang immediately led senior police officers to the scene and arrested the two men. One claimed to be Wu Jiamo, from Danyang, whose father, Wu Yuankai, had previously served as the military governor of Hubei. The other claimed to be Zhang Deshun, from Huizhou, a wounded soldier from the Second Army Hospital. Fake seals, inspection certificates, and opium red pills were found on them. Officer Wang suspected them and took them to the bureau for investigation. The Provincial Government Orders the Removal of the Reflection Wall at Xuanmiao Temple The County Government received an order from the Provincial Government regarding the demolition of the reflection wall at Xuanmiao Temple and has instructed the Construction Department to follow the original plan. Bao Gujia, Fan Junbo, and others telegraphed the National Government's Ministry of the Interior, the Provincial Government, and the County Government, requesting that it be preserved and that the execution be halted.

False Alarm on the Night Express Train The Shanghai-Nanjing Railway’s twenty-seventh night express train departed from the North Station at around 11:00 PM the other day (the 7th), carrying the President of the Executive Yuan, Tan Yankai, and the Minister of Railways, Sun Ke. At 1:05 AM yesterday morning, it arrived at Suzhou Station and then headed north. Near Railway No. 116 and telegraph pole No. 94.19 near Huguan, it was stopped and dense gunfire was heard. Although the lights of the train head were visible from Huguan Station, the police force was small and it was inconvenient to go and investigate due to the gunfire. At 1:30 AM, when the second night express train arrived in Suzhou from Shanghai, Suzhou Station had not yet received a report that the twenty-seventh train had reached Huguan Station. It immediately sent a telegram to inquire, but the telegraph and telephone lines between Suzhou and Huguan were suddenly out of service. Another line was used to relay the inquiry from Mangting to Huguan. As the truth was unknown, Station Master Huang Jiaxiong reported that the twenty-seventh train was stopped there, fearing an accident. He immediately telegraphed the General Station's Vehicle Department and requested that the military police be dispatched. A platoon of military police stationed in Suzhou, accompanied by road police officers and laborers, took a push car to investigate. They found that telegraph pole No. 19 had been destroyed and had fallen on the railway, but there was nothing else. The telegraph pole was removed, and at around 4:00 AM, the train safely proceeded. The second train departed from Suzhou to Nanjing at 4:30 AM.

Local People Appointed as Antiquities Preservation Committee Members Chen Dingxiang, Chen Xuehai, and Xu Xiang were appointed as members of the Jiangsu Antiquities Preservation Committee yesterday.

Large Band of Bandits Arrived at Sijing Port The County Government yesterday (the 7th) received a telegram from the Public Security Bureau stating that the county head of Wu County, Huang Junjian, had received an urgent telegram from Ma, the captain of the Xietang Town police company, reporting that large groups of bandits, numbering four to five hundred, had arrived at Zhou Chen Sijing Port, Longting and Panlongpu. They were armed with guns and weapons and were extremely dangerous due to the small police force, requesting aid. In addition to the telegrams to the brigade headquarters, special telegram was issued. Zou Jing, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, kowtowed. After receiving the telegram, County Head Huang immediately ordered the 1st platoon of the 1st Company to go and pursue the bandits.

Fengxian

County Government Thoroughly Investigating Reactionary Elements in the Police Force County Head Shen Qingchen recently received reports that some unscrupulous elements in the county police force have been incited by reactionary factions from the north and have accepted false commissions, plotting to create disturbances. After careful investigation and confirmation, he ordered Public Security Bureau Chief Li Zhiwu and Acting Police Captain Tu Qin to dispatch capable teams to monitor the actions in various sub-bureaus without raising any alarms. The team leaders and police officers who are heavily suspected were arrested and investigated. In the past two days, five or six people have been identified and are being interrogated. But the details are being kept secret, so it is difficult to obtain any information.

Wuxi

Record of the General Meeting of the Cocoon Industry Association Because the autumn cocoons are about to hit the market, the Cocoon Industry Association needed to discuss fresh cocoon prices and opening dates in advance. It specially convened a general meeting of all businesses yesterday, attended by more than 130 people. It was decided: (1) Each business can purchase goods on the opening date; (2) The cocoon price should be at most 50 yuan, with subsequent reductions.

Reasons for the Rise and Fall of Rice Prices Rice prices in Wuxi have been soaring recently due to continuous rain and interrupted supplies. New white rice rose to 19 yuan per dan, causing panic among the common people. It is now known that 800 tons of new rice have arrived the day before, so white rice prices on the market fell by three yuan yesterday, to 16 yuan per dan. However, there are no supplies of new white indica (i.e., Bianjiang indica) and new guest rice, so rice prices are expected to remain high. New white indica is priced at 11.10 to 10.10 yuan per dan, and new guest rice is 5.40 to 4.80 yuan per dan. But wheat sales are sluggish, at 8.15 yuan per dan. The price of old broken rice is very high, at 17.20 yuan per dan. It is said that a large batch of Shanghai indica and large-grain indica rice (which can replace old broken rice) will arrive in Wuxi for sale within the next few days. If the supply of rice from all sources is steady, rice prices should fall.

Representatives of Private Electrical Companies Visit Wuxi Li Yanshi (manager of the Huzhou Electrical Company), the chief representative of the China Private Electrical Companies Association, arrived in Wuxi by train from Shanghai at about 9 PM the other day. Yesterday he visited the Wuxi office of the Liu Fu Qishuyan Power Plant. Director Wu and the head of the office, Zhu Zhilun, gave him a warm welcome. Mr. Li also reported on the key points regarding the necessary equipment and improvements for the electrical industry at the Power Conference. In the afternoon, he visited the power plant in Qishuyan and then went to Suzhou, Changzhou, and Zhenjiang to visit.

Wuxi-Chengjiang Ferry Boat Robbed at Night There is a night ferry boat running between Wuxi and Yuecheng Bridge in Jiangyin, owned by Wang Xiaohai and Jin Jugen. It has been quite peaceful every day. But yesterday, the ferry boat was sailing from the countryside to Wuxi. At about 3:00 AM, it suddenly encountered a pirate ship in the Dawanli area. Seven or eight pirates, armed with handguns and flashlights, ordered the boat to stop. They swarmed onto the boat, first firing two shots into the air to show their power, and then began to loot. All the passengers on the boat were searched. After half an hour, they left with their loot. A total of 80 yuan in silver dollars, three pecks of white rice, a bundle of clothes, and a pair of gold rings were stolen, for a total loss of 289 yuan.

Changzhou

Measures to Deal with Captured Bandits Have Been Determined After the military and police of Wu and Danyang launched a major campaign to suppress bandits in the border area and captured many bandit leaders, Corps Commander Wu Chengren and County Head Wu Deyuan went to Shanghai to see Commander Xiong and report on the progress of the bandit suppression. After Corps Commander Wu and County Head Wu returned to Changzhou, they were summoned to Shanghai by Commander Xiong on the 5th and returned to Changzhou on the afternoon of the 7th. It was heard that Commander Xiong had given instructions on how to deal with the bandits, and there were also instructions on how to deal with the captured bandits. In the future, the arrest of bandits can be handled more decisively.

The Weitang Ferry Boat Robbed En Route The Weitang ferry boat of Wu County was sailing from Baizhang to Changzhou on the evening of the 5th. When it reached Xingcun Bridge, six or seven robbers suddenly appeared. They were armed with handguns and spoke with a northern accent. They boarded the ship and robbed the passengers and crew, taking everything of value. More than 500 yuan was lost. After the robbery, they went to the northwest.

Nantong

Headquarters Commend Wounded Soldiers The General Headquarters dispatched Dai Mingxin and others to Tong to commend the wounded soldiers of the 31st Rear Hospital. The roll call of soldiers and patients was held at 7 PM. Soldiers were given 10 yuan each, lieutenants 30 yuan, and field officers 100 yuan. In addition to those who had already received the commendation at the front, more than 1,100 wounded soldiers and patients in Tong received the awards.

Marine Corps in Charge of City Defense The Marine Corps landed and was stationed in the city to take charge of security for a week. The Hai Chou warship, which was ordered to sail to Shanghai on the 11th, will be replaced by a team from the Hai Rong warship.

Request to Allocate Funds for the Rear Hospital Dean Cao of the hospital telegraphed Army Medical Director Jiang to urgently allocate funds for the rear hospital. The telegram read: "The hospital only received 1,690 yuan this month. Due to your telegram, local authorities have refused to lend money. If the food supply is cut off and other changes occur, how will I maintain the hospital? Please remit the funds on time and also issue the funds for July and August so that the local authorities can be repaid."

Bandit Army Occupies Xidang in the Reclamation Area The northern Jiangsu Suyang River southern reclamation area has been disturbed by Ma Yuren colluding with bandits. The bandits have set up a false headquarters in Xiwu, and they are very rampant. All the employees and tenants of the eleven large and small salt reclamation companies in the vicinity have fled.

Change of Education Bureau Director Song Bingong, Director of the Nantong County Education Bureau, has resigned. The Department of Education has appointed Guan Jincheng, the Chief of General Affairs of the Bureau, as acting director.

Gaoyou

Record of the Trial of the Bandit Collusion Case Wang Zhou, a widow from Lingtang Bridge in Huxi, belonging to the county, had a son, who was eight years old. Last winter, he was kidnapped by bandits and redeemed this spring. Wang Zhou suspected Lin Yuwen of colluding with the bandits, so she filed a lawsuit with the county government. Yesterday (the 6th) at 3:00 PM, the original plaintiff, the defendant, and witnesses were summoned to court. The judge, Hu Cheng, opened the court for trial. Wang Zhou testified that last winter, many bandits suddenly came, smashed open the gate, and armed with guns, broke into the house and tied her up. One bandit guarded her, while the rest rushed into the bedroom and searched everywhere, but found nothing. Then they kidnapped her young son. Less than a month later, she received a letter from the bandits asking her to prepare 2,000 yuan and contact Lin Yuwen. She borrowed 1,500 yuan from relatives and friends and invited her clan member Wang Baohua to contact Lin. The next day, her son was released. According to Lin Yuwen's testimony, there was no redemption ticket. Wang Baohua, the witness, confronted him, and Lin Yuwen had no way to deny it. It was proven that Wang Baohua smoked opium, and Judge Hu ordered Wang Zhou to return. Lin Yuwen was suspected of colluding with the bandits, and was taken into custody for investigation, and to be punished according to the law if the investigation is true. Wang Baohua was sent to the Zhongqiu Hospital for a three-day test by the police.

Rugao

Piracy in Juegang is Extremely Rampant Jin Zhipeng, who lives in Huanbeizui, near Changsha Town in the Juegang District of this county, has a well-to-do family. At about 1:00 AM on the 30th of last month, more than 40 pirates suddenly came, armed with box guns and flashlights. They broke into the house, overturned the boxes, and searched everywhere, causing a loss of more than 500 yuan. Jin Zihenglian ran away and was shot in the leg by the bandits. After the robbery, they kidnapped Jin Sun Erhou (16 years old) and Sanhou (9 years old). Yesterday (the 4th), many pirates set fire to six fishing boats belonging to Chen Shuzhai, Xing Jinwen, Li Er, etc. The fire lit up the sky for three hours before it was extinguished. On the 26th of last month, a merchant ship named San Hexing, led by Cao Jianshu and sixteen crew members including Wang Zhengcai and Guo Chuncai, went to sea to fish. They had just left the port when they encountered more than ten pirates who boarded the boat with weapons. Six people were tricked and forced to get off the boat, and Wang Zhengcai and the other ten people were forced to sail north. Their whereabouts are still unknown, and their families are extremely anxious.

Zhenjiang

Banditry Rampant in the Countryside Banditry is rampant in Zhenjiang's countryside, and robberies are frequently heard, making it difficult for people to sleep peacefully. Yesterday, more than 20 bandits suddenly came to Zhoucun, carrying weapons, surrounded the village, and demanded 1,000 yuan in support, otherwise they would burn the village. The villagers were shocked. After the security teams of the neighboring villages arrived after hearing the alarm, the bandits left, shouting and screaming. Before leaving, they burned six or seven thatched houses on the east side of the village. The village has telegraphed the province requesting troops for protection. Also, a family in Hanjia Village outside the South Gate received a letter from the bandits a few days ago, ordering them to pay 25,800 yuan. The village has not yet come up with a response. Also, eight bandits armed with guns came to Xilu Village in the southern countryside and attacked the village, robbing it. The village security team worked hard to resist and opened fire, and the bandits retreated. Wu Chengyang, the chief of the Third District, has reported the situation to the county government and requested that the security office dispatch a battalion of troops to be stationed in Shangdang Xilu area for suppression. Also, there are frequent ticket scams in villages such as Shenggan Xiwannan Gang in the southern countryside, and the villagers cannot live in peace. For days, they have been bringing their old and young to the city to seek refuge. According to the investigation, there are about more than one thousand people.

Two Sugar Stores Close Down One After Another Zhenjiang's commerce has been very depressed in recent years due to various reasons. As a result, many businesses have suffered losses. Last month, Tao Liji Tung Oil Store in Yao Yiwan went bankrupt with more than 70,000 yuan in debt, which has not yet been settled. Yesterday, Yongyu Sugar Store and Qingtai Chang Sugar Store in Yao Yiwan went bankrupt one after another due to poor cash flow. It is reported that Yongyu owes more than 76,000 yuan and Qingtai Chang owes more than 58,500 yuan, mostly loans from Zhenjiang's money houses. The money houses are very panicked by this blow and are paying close attention to their loans. The market has suddenly become tense. However, the shareholders of Qingtai Chang are all wealthy and plan to raise capital to maintain operations.

Yangzhou

A Dispute Between an Uncle and Nephew Results in Death Zheng Meixian, a farmer from the Hebei area of the first bridge of the Xiannv Temple, in the county, had a dispute with his uncle, Naifu, a few days ago due to a certain incident. At first, they quarreled, and then they fought. After being persuaded by neighbors, the two parties agreed to go to the Deyuelou teahouse in Xianzhen to settle the matter. However, Naifu, still unwilling, secretly asked someone to report to the 4th Sub-Bureau of the Public Security Bureau, who sent the police to detain both the plaintiff and the defendant. Officer Dai of the bureau interrogated them and sentenced them to several days of detention for violating the police law. But one wave subsided, and another rose. Meixian's father, Nailian, believed that his cousin, Nailu, had instigated the quarrel and the arrest. So he led his wife and his 80-year-old mother to Nailu's house to make a fuss. The Public Security Sub-Bureau again summoned both parties to the case. The testimonies were very harsh. The bureau prepared a document and sent the police to escort them to the city and send them to the county court for punishment. Nailian's mother heard about the matter, and was worried that her son and grandson had been detained. At the same time, she was old and deaf. When she walked to the river near her home, she suddenly lost her footing, fell into the water, and drowned. Then Nailian's wife carried her mother-in-law's body to Nailu's house, saying that her mother-in-law had been secretly beaten to death by Nailu. Therefore, both parties filed a lawsuit with the court based on their reasons, requesting that the court handle it according to law.

Changshu

Resolution to Request the Closure of Ayu Estuary Ayu Estuary, under the jurisdiction of the first district in the county, is an important passage from Yangcheng Lake to the various sea ports of Hupu, Xuliujing, and Gaopu Estuary. Two years ago, the band of bandits from Sang Hai Shan entered Yangcheng Lake via Hupu through the Estuary, a necessary route for bandits. Now, cases of kidnapping are happening frequently, and the atmosphere is not peaceful. Zhang Jiashen and others, the town head of the second district of Zhendong Town, proposed at the eleventh district meeting that the county magistrate and the first district office be asked to implement the closure of Ayu Estuary. It was resolved to submit the proposal to the county for approval by the district office.

New Director of Finance Bureau Arrives in Chang The previous report mentioned that Fei Yuhong, the director of the county's finance bureau, and Hao Bingzhang, the director of the Gaoyou County bureau, would be transferred to each other. It is now known that the new director, Hao Bingzhang, arrived in Chang on the morning of the 7th by the Kunshan ferry. He will take over the office on the 8th and officially take office on the 11th.

Jiashan

Details of the Suppression Following the Robbery of Oil Carts in Tianning On the morning of the 7th, bandits (mixed from Taibao, Ashu, Henan, and Haizhou gangs) who had fled to Taozhuang invaded Tianning Village (under the jurisdiction of Jiashan) and Youche Port (under the jurisdiction of Jiaxing) and engaged in looting. They confiscated the weapons of the Baoqu Corps. The telephone line from Tianning Village to Jiashan City was cut. After the incident, Jiaxing was informed by telegraph from Youche Port. The Jiahu Bandit Suppression Headquarters immediately telegraphed the Jiashan Security Team, the Xitang Water Police 8th Team, and the Pingyao Water Police 7th Team, to encircle them separately. The Xitang 8th Team and the Patrol Team went on the Zhi Guo warship. They encountered six or seventy bandit ships with more than 400 bandits in Jiangcun Xiaogang. They immediately attacked head-on. The bandits stubbornly resisted and fired machine guns. The warship fired its cannons for cover. The fierce battle lasted three hours. Fortunately, reinforcements arrived, and the bandits retreated to Xiamu Marsh and Fenhu Lake. Two bandits were killed, more than twenty were injured, and three guns were captured. Three members of the Patrol Team were injured. In the evening, the entire team returned to the 8th Team headquarters in Xitang, carrying the bodies of the bandits. It was rumored that they would be beheaded and displayed in the area where the incident occurred. When the bandits invaded the two towns, stray bullets flew, wounding eight or nine men and women, including Zhu Jinsheng. It was heard that when the Jiashan Ganya reinforcements arrived, the bandits had already retreated. The Shan Li and Shan Tian ferries were prepared for bandit suppression. The passengers were driven off, and it is difficult to restore the original state today. The county government will conduct an inspection this afternoon.

Hangzhou

Most of the Loans Secured Because the Zhejiang Provincial Government's treasury was depleted and urgently needed funds, it planned to borrow one million yuan for relief. After consulting with the leaders of the Hangzhou silver and money industries, the two industries worked together to contribute 500,000 yuan each. A contract was signed the other day, and the funds have been transferred to the provincial treasury for use. As for the deficit, it will be borrowed from Ningbo and other places. A telegram was sent to the Ningbo Municipal Government and the county governments of neighboring counties to borrow 250,000 yuan from the silver and money industries. To be cautious, the former director of the neighboring county's general donation bureau, Zhu Luzhong, was specially appointed as a liaison officer and rushed to Ningbo to discuss the matter.

The Gan Bandits Retreat to Shangrao River Estuary The Zhejiang Provincial Government received a telegram from Guangfeng Xingchang on the 7th, stating that the Zeng bandits who had been defeated before had come back. The situation was critical, and they requested that troops be dispatched to encircle and suppress them. After receiving the telegram, the Provincial Government immediately dispatched Zhao Junmai, the head of the training regiment, to Gan, splitting the forces to attack from different directions. One force attacked from the front, while another force took a roundabout route behind the bandits. The bandit forces were unable to hold out and retreated to the Shangrao River Estuary. Many weapons were seized, and many bandits were captured. The area around Changshan is now relatively peaceful.

Educational News Highlights

Ministry of Education Requests Allocation of Funds for National Schools

Will Submit a Proposal to the Executive Yuan Meeting to Raise Funds for One Month

According to the Central News Agency, funds for national schools in Beijing, Shanghai, Tianjin, and other places have been in arrears for many months. Even the funds for May of this year have not been fully allocated. Currently, the schools are preparing to start the semester and urgently need funds. The schools have been sending telegrams to the Ministry of Education to urge the allocation of funds for maintenance. The Ministry of Education has been unable to cope with this problem. It is now planning to propose at the Executive Yuan meeting that the Ministry of Finance investigate the outstanding funds for each school and quickly allocate funds for one month for relief. It is reported that Jiang Menglin, the Minister of Education, has prepared two proposals and has submitted them to the Executive Yuan to be placed on the agenda of the Executive Yuan meeting for discussion. China

The Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society is Actively Being Prepared

Members Register in Succession

Issue Half-Price Train Tickets

The Seventh Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society is scheduled to be held in Wuxi from September 20th. The progress of the preparations has been reported in this newspaper. The following are further details.

Members Continue to Register As of the 5th, the Preparatory Committee has received continued registration from members including Shao Yuanchong of the Examination Yuan, Dai Mingli of the Ministry of Finance, Chen Gongda of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, Chen Zhenyi and Li Zhaohuan of the Ministry of Railways, and Chen Changtong of the Shanghai Bank of China, totaling 100 people, including 46 family members.

Distribute Train Tickets After receiving the replies from the registered members, the Preparatory Committee contacted the Railway Bureau for group half-price train tickets, which have been arranged. The tickets have been distributed to the members so that they can take the train to Wuxi to attend the meeting at that time.

Banquet Locations Finalized The Society has a total of 350 members. Although not all of them will be able to attend the annual meeting, the number of people coming to Wuxi, including family members, may not be small. There are no large banquet halls in Wuxi, so the Preparatory Committee was very hesitant. It has now been decided to use three locations: the County Chamber of Commerce Hall, the New World Hall, and the Mei Garden. The banquet dates have also been arranged. The first day is for the County Chamber of Commerce and other merchant groups, the second day is for the silver and money industry, the third day is for educational institutions, and the fourth day is for a return banquet for the Society. Pan Gengsheng, the newly appointed County Head of Wuxi and a member of the Society, also plans to host a banquet for the members, but the banquet dates have already been reserved, so it is quite difficult to arrange. It will probably only be possible to hold a joint banquet with other institutions and groups.

Local Municipal Education Bureau

Popular Education and Supplementary School Promotion Plan

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education has announced the popular education and supplementary school promotion plan for the 19th year. The details are as follows: (A) Popular Education Schools, (1) Two Central Popular Education Schools, (1) The First Central Popular Education School is located at the Minglun Hall, Wenmiao Road, Hunan, Shanghai. (2) The Second Central Popular Education School is located at the Pingmin Residence, Jinjia Lane, Zhabei. (Description) Each school has three classes: morning, half-day, and evening, with a study period of five months. The principal is responsible for guiding all administrative and teaching matters in the district's popular education schools and also serves as the morning class teacher and handles all administrative affairs within the school. One teacher is responsible for the school's academic affairs. (2) Seventy district popular education schools. (1) Fifty schools will be opened in the first half of the year, including eight in the Hunan district, ten in the Zhabei district, seven in the Pusong district, two in the Yangjing district, two in the Yangsi district, one in the Gaoxing district, three in the Luxing district, two in the Caojing district, two in the Tangqiao district, two in the Yinxiang district, one in the Fahua district, two in the Gaoqiao district, one in the Zhenru district, one in the Pengpu district, two in the Wusong district, two in the Jiangwan district, and two in the Yinhang district. New Plans After the Patriotic Girls' School Relocates

Since the Patriotic Girls' School moved to the Chen Garden on Jiangwan Road, the new school building has been beautifully landscaped with flowers and trees. The location is quiet and ideal for studying, a far cry from the old site in Tianbao Lane. This semester, there are more than 250 boarding students, and about 100 day students find the transportation convenient. Currently, the senior high school department is headed by Sun Xiangzhong and Yin Songyai, and the junior high school department is headed by Li Chucai. The heads of each department are all experienced. The school library has always had more than 10,000 books. Recently, to benefit the many boarding students, it plans to purchase the "Wan You Wen Ku" (Universal Library) for reading. As for the physical education department, starting this semester, the graduation period will be changed to three years in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry of Education. The qualifications of admitted students are also limited to junior high school graduates. The sports field and covered playground are being constructed on rented nearby vacant land, and bidding is currently underway.

Jinan University Held Opening Ceremony Yesterday

National Jinan University held its autumn semester opening ceremony at 8:00 AM yesterday in the Zhiyuan Hall. Nearly a thousand people attended, including the president, vice president, deans of various colleges, department heads, professors, lecturers, middle school teachers, office staff, and new and old students from both the university and middle school divisions. The ceremony began with music played by the Western orchestra, followed by the customary formalities. President Zheng gave a speech: (1) He elaborated on the significance of overseas Chinese education and the university's educational policy. (2) He encouraged students to first focus on basic science and then specialize in the study of overseas Chinese culture in order to make a contribution. (3) He mentioned that the university's finances have been declining since the reorganization, but construction has continued. Although the university has received much praise from the public, he personally felt that it was still not satisfactory and would strive to expand the library, purchase equipment, and improve facilities in the future. (4) He emphasized the improvement of the middle school division and the streamlining of academic affairs. (5) He stipulated that students must adhere to standards and avoid waste in annual expenses. (6) He expressed the hope that those in charge of physical education and Boy Scout training would actively take responsibility. (7) He emphasized the importance of discipline. Finally, he expressed gratitude to the teachers on behalf of the students' parents and entrusted them with the responsibility of sincerely teaching and guiding their children. Subsequently, Shen Yizhen, the new director of the middle school division, delivered a speech: (1) He emphasized the importance of having a spirit of inquiry in learning. (2) He emphasized the importance of having a sense of love for the group. (3) He emphasized the importance of having a peaceful attitude in dealing with people and affairs. He also stated that the advantages of overseas Chinese students are their straightforwardness, lack of deceitful behavior, lively demeanor, lack of rigidity, and strong emotions. He hoped that they would continue to maintain these strengths and develop them further. After the music was played, the ceremony was declared complete.

Both men and women are welcome, and anyone with a sincere love for painting can join the research at any time during the period.

Wang Yunwu Dictionary Gains Popularity in Middle Schools

Since Wang Yunwu invented the Four-Corner Numeral System, various institutions, schools, and individuals at home and abroad have competed to adopt it because it is easy to learn and use. Recently, Mr. Wang has further compiled the "Wang Yunwu's Great Dictionary" according to the order of the four-corner codes, so that the reading public can use the simplest indexing method to obtain the most applicable reference book. The content of the book encompasses encyclopedic knowledge and meets the latest needs. Its level is suitable for general application, especially for middle school students. Many middle schools near and far have adopted it as a standard reference book. Zheng Tonghe, the principal of a Shanghai middle school, praised it as "(the materials are well-chosen, the explanations are clear, and it is compiled and arranged according to the four-corner numeral indexing method, making it easy to check. It is truly a scientific dictionary.)" The comments of secondary educators on this book are evident here.

"Outline of Historical Studies" by Lu Shaoji Published

The two books "Three Principles of the People Education Law" and "Outline of Historical Studies," both written by Mr. Lu Shaoji, the head of the normal school department and history of education teacher at the Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai Middle School in this city, are published by the Commercial Press. "Three Principles of the People Education Law" was published in the fall of the year before last and has already been reprinted. "Outline of Historical Studies" has now also been published, with a real price of sixty cents. The book first discusses what history is and what historiography is, then describes the history of Chinese historiography and the history of Western historiography, then discusses the relationship between historiography and science, and finally elaborates on historical research methods and teaching methods. The main aim is to instill in readers the common sense of historiography and to point out the path of historical research. The narration is concise and the arguments are precise, which is very convenient for beginners. Before publication, it was proofread by the contemporary historians He Bingsong and Fu Yunsen, and it received high praise from both gentlemen. Those teaching high school or university (General History) for one semester can adopt it as a textbook, and those studying history can also use it as a reference.

Chinese football and basketball teams to compete with the University of the Philippines during the Philippine Carnival next spring, and form a women's track and field team to compete with Filipino female athletes. Robert Cup Preliminary Round

China Straight Wins over Japan Three Times

Lin and Qiu's Skills are Superb

The Shanghai International Tennis Robert Cup preliminary round, which has been postponed repeatedly, was finally held at the Chinese Tennis Court yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM thanks to good weather. Chinese tennis stars Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai interacted with Japanese representatives Okamoto and Matsunaga. After three to five rounds, the superiority of the two sides became clear. Soon, Lin and Qiu won with a clean sweep of three wins, which was heard in the field.

Ten Minutes to Win a Set

Lin and Qiu's victory was due to their high skills and was by no means a fluke. However, the first set was the most impressive of the three sets won. The six games of the set were almost entirely dominated by Lin and Qiu. The opponent could only run left and right according to the direction of their rackets. Lin and Qiu's attacking methods each had their own brilliant points, and this set was particularly colorful. In ten minutes, they defeated their opponents, resulting in a 6-0 victory in the first set. Nothing could be faster than this.

Loose Formation in the Last Two Sets

In the second and third sets, Lin and Qiu were more lenient and gave their opponents more room to move around. Therefore, the formation of the two sides was somewhat loose. In the first two games of the second set, Lin and Qiu's line was not solid, so Matsunaga made two counter-draws, creating an advantage, and the victory went to the Japanese. But after three to three, Lin and Qiu rallied and finally won the second set 6-3. The number of wins for Lin and Qiu in the third set was the same as in the second set, but the difference was that Lin and Qiu were at a 4-1 advantage, and the Japanese became very active, their sharpness was irresistible for a time, and soon the score became 5-3 (China took the lead). After this, although the Japanese wanted to speed up, Lin and Qiu resolutely added a vicious blow, adding one more game and completing the whole effort.

China Lin Baohua Qiu Feihai 6 0 6 3 6 3 Okamoto Matsunaga

Free Talk

A Word of Insight

— Wang Shouyang

The way people view themselves often errs on the side of arrogance or humility. The reason for the emergence of arrogance and humility mostly lies in the presence of a comparative mind.

The more intelligent and wise a person is, the easier it is for them to commit evil. The more foolish and dull-witted a person is, the more difficult it is for them to achieve anything.

Whether life has a purpose or not is a philosophical question. But without a purpose, there is no meaning. And with a purpose, it is impossible to say what it is.

People often suffer from a sense of inadequacy. But under this concept, they can create or destroy careers, reach a state of high intelligence, and descend into a state of baseness.

Young people find the words of their parents, no matter how good or medicinal, difficult to hear. But they treat the words of their wives, no matter how trivial, as golden rules.

Do not blame others for your mistakes, thinking you have gained an advantage. Beware that others may blame you for their mistakes.

The great French writer Victor Hugo said, "The present world should not be called the world, but the pit of hatred." How painful his words are.

Things that are difficult to obtain are all excellent wishes. But when wishes are fulfilled, the heart becomes indifferent. All the non-thoughts of people should be viewed as fulfilled wishes, then the world will be full of good people.

Ordinary people cultivate themselves and find interest in their own realm of thought and joy in it. Conversely, the pleasure of mediocre people is always sought outside themselves, so they are often dissatisfied and in pain.

In Remembrance of Teacher Zeng Nongran

— Zhang Shanzi

After the national upheaval, Teacher Zeng Nongran took refuge on the sea, supporting himself by selling calligraphy and paintings alongside Teacher Li Mei'an of Linchuan, a figure known as 'Zeng Li' by the world. The passing of Teacher Mei deeply saddened him. As the world grew more chaotic and his desire to return home remained unfulfilled, he once painted a landscape on Buddha's Birthday, inscribing it with the words: "To wander where Yangzi [Yang Xiong] wandered, one grows old. To wander where Mozi wandered, one becomes a Buddha. The world is muddled; to whom shall I return? The mountains and rivers are vast; who is their master? My brush creates as it pleases, as if after the primeval chaos. I do this for self-amusement, not daring to seek recognition." From this, one can glimpse his solitary and independent spirit. Yet, his mind grew stronger with age. Seated at his desk, brush in hand, he never seemed to tire. During his brief rests, he would discuss calligraphy and painting with his disciples, critiquing poetry and prose. My eighth brother, Daqian, and I often visited, deepening our bond. This year, in the fifth month, as I approached my forty-ninth year, the Teacher gifted me a couplet: "Brothers in advanced years, like Wen Bozi; in poetry, calligraphy, and painting, like Su Changgong." While I am ashamed to be called exceeding my ability, I indeed see the earnest encouragement. I also saw the Teacher newly painted a fan for Old Man Wei Ruosou, inscribing it with the words: "One must reach a hundred years without the aura of old age; together, let us enjoy the six principles [of painting] like enjoying naturalness." He further wrote on another side: "The will commands the energy; therefore, it is the will that masters the energy of morning and evening. To seek ease in youth and indulge in idleness in adulthood is the aura of old age. Mr. Xi and Mr. A-ge are both seventy years old. Mr. A-ge still engages with the world through calligraphy and painting. Mr. Xi never ceases writing and painting, even in the height of summer; that is the aura of morning." On the painting, he added, "I wish to confirm this with Mr. A-ge." Wei Ruosou was from the same hometown and the same year as the Teacher and studied together. Ruosou was one day older, so the Teacher treated him as an elder brother. I said that the Teacher's aura of morning would last forever, reaching the longevity of a great catalpa tree. Unexpectedly, he fell slightly ill in the autumn and passed away. Four days before his passing, he still wrote a poem for Old Man Wu Jianqiu: "Since the Jue Stream flows, it always winds around the pavilion; the willows planted by hand have already formed a dike. After the catastrophe, there is still my humble cottage; how sad that I cannot return home year after year." According to this poem, it was inscribed on the 'Thinking of Home' painting, which was made for Ruosou. His soul still yearned for his homeland; this can be seen here. Jianweng was also the Teacher's old friend of thirty years. When the Teacher was ill, he moved his bed to the Teacher's house. One day, the Teacher suddenly became unhappy and said to Jianweng, "At seventy-three years old, in this troubled time, to have a friend like you, a cry over my coffin, what more could I regret in death?" His voice was sorrowful and resonant, his emotions profound. Therefore, Jianweng lamented the Teacher, saying, "What is life for? To witness this land filled with desolation. Now he is truly dead, yet there is still one who cries over his coffin." Alas! The Teacher's calligraphy and painting already fill the world. The Teacher's fame will surely flow to later generations. He returned in full age; though dead, he is still alive. The feeling of the mountain collapsing and the tree decaying cannot be dispelled from our hearts. In the autumn sun of the Yangtze and Han Rivers, I wish to recite this with all his disciples. (Jue Chou)

Teacher Zeng's Remaining Works

Balsam of Xiangtan, Woody Variety

— Yimei

"Nine colors of spring hues gather together, a splendid grace of Phoenix presence." This is a beautiful verse by Yan Shu praising the balsam flower. Balsam is an herbaceous plant, with stems about a foot high. It blooms in early autumn, displaying a dazzling array of colors. In the old days, women often picked them to dye their nails. This was also a charming pastime in boudoirs. Recently, a friend named Fang Zibaochu, a native of Xiangtan, described the balsam in his family's Fragrant Neighbor Cottage. It is more than ten feet tall, with deep red flowers, just like the herbaceous variety. The leaves are also similar to the usual kind. From early autumn to mid-winter, it blooms continuously for five months. The seeds are as hard as iron. When scattered elsewhere, they do not sprout. Therefore, there is no second such plant in Xiangzhong. Zibaochu's father, Suisheng, enjoyed planting flowers and trees in his leisure time and found pleasure in watering and weeding. One autumn day, the balsam was in full bloom. Suddenly, a storm arose, with lightning striking. One of the balsam's stems was cut off from the root. No attention was paid to it. The next day, a sprout grew from the stem, gradually growing taller and taller, amazingly transforming from a herb into a woody plant. Suisheng believed this to be a sign of good fortune. He built a Woody Balsam Pavilion beside it as a place for relaxing and enjoying himself. It has been more than ten years since then. It blooms once a year and has not yet withered.

A Scene in a Trash Can

— Zui Chisheng

The trash can, although a place for concealing filth, also contains a sense of mystery. Therefore, sometimes love letters are found, scraps of silk. Those who find them often feel that there is a special charm. But this is just the beginning of a heterosexual love affair. There are also those who have been through the battlefield of love, conceived unwanted pregnancies, and given birth to unofficial crystallized products. Unable to deal with them, they often wrap them in a cloth and secretly abandon them in the trash can. Some are still alive, others already dead. We can often see or hear about this strange phenomenon in the streets and alleys of civilized cities. As for asking who manufactured this, who abandoned it, it is impossible to pursue. So this trash can is simply a (mystery vault.) Who knows how many romances and tragedies it contains.

It is said that one afternoon, I was going to Nanshi for a consultation. While passing by a trash can near Wangjia Wharf, there was a crowd of people gathered around. Driven by curiosity, I joined the spectators. It turned out that there was a cloth bundle in the trash can, containing a (male) infant who had already died. It was padded with lime. The skin was rosy and the body was plump, different from ordinary children. The skull had been smashed, the brains splattered. The face was a bloody mess, a horrific sight. There is no doubt that this was an illegitimate child, killed and then abandoned. Among the onlookers, some were shaking their heads and sighing, others were cursing loudly. After seeing it, I also felt endless emotions. If this baby had been born into a wealthy family or a normal family without children, what joy it would have brought. And it would have been held with infinite hope. But it was born of an improper union. What is called (hatred wishes it dead) was carried out, and it was put to death. It is pitiful that, ignorant and unknowing, it suffered such cruel treatment, ending its short life, and no one cries injustice for it. This is truly the most unfair thing in the world. Therefore, from a legal perspective, it should be punished. Because it concerns human life, it also has value to investigate thoroughly. There is another aspect. I hope that local people, when an illegitimate child is born, bawling as it falls to the ground, surely someone will know. But there are also those who are suffocated at the time. It is appropriate to provide guidance or warnings beforehand. If nursing is inconvenient, instruct them to send it to an orphanage. Do not abandon it arbitrarily. The Health Bureau or the Women and Children Relief Association should best establish several regulations to ensure that the average illegitimate infant receives a measure of life protection. In the future, they can also gain a foothold in society. This is truly a matter of concern in the discussion of humanitarianism.

A Record of Obsessive Devotion

— Chen Boying

Zhao Zhong, a native of Wuxian, had handsome features and a love for literature and art, but was slow to speak, stammering when he tried to speak. One evening, when he was just over twenty years old, he was watching a play at the New Stage when he saw a woman in a box. Her hair was like dark clouds, her clothes were a honey-colored long skirt, and she wore a light red half-sleeved jacket. Her eyes were clear like autumn water. Zhao Zhong was amazed, thinking her a celestial being, and he gazed at her without shifting his eyes. When the curtain fell, Zhao Zhong rushed to the door to wait for her. He saw the woman leaving with a companion, and suddenly she smiled, her teeth like rows of shells, white and unmatched. Zhao Zhong felt as if his soul had left his body. The woman left the door, got into a car, and drove away. Zhao Zhong quickly hailed a streetcar to follow her. The woman arrived at her residence, entered the door, and closed it. Zhao Zhong then noted the number of the door and returned. The woman's surname was Zhang, her given name was Caiqin, and she was from Hangzhou. Her father was a wealthy merchant. At that time, she was studying at a certain girls' school. That evening, she had not seen Zhao Zhong at all. Her smile was due to her companion's joke about a comical part in the play. Therefore, she could not help but smile, for no other reason. From that day on, Zhao Zhong waited for her on his bicycle, but he never saw her. A doctor lived with the woman in her residence. Zhao Zhong pretended to be a patient seeking medical attention and went there many times, but he never caught a glimpse of her. After several months of this, Zhao Zhong's longing grew even stronger. However, Caiqin did not know anything about it. At that time, there was a great epidemic. Caiqin died and her coffin was placed in a temple. Zhao Zhong was often seen placing a bouquet of flowers in front of the coffin every day. Since the woman's death, Zhao Zhong had been depressed and unhappy. Within a month, he was coughing up blood and died. After his death, the two families gradually investigated the reason and felt sorry for Zhao Zhong's infatuation and grieved for his short-lived love. They then held a ghost marriage.

Internal Politics of Post-War Poland (2)

— Li Liuzeng, Sent from Paris

Under these circumstances, the first step taken by the Provisional Government was to convene a constitutional assembly. However, even before the assembly was established, the Provisional Government had already issued a variety of orders. The most important of these included the recognition of an eight-hour workday, mandatory epidemic prevention laws, and compulsory education. In addition, there were clear regulations regarding labor supervision, labor unions, and the requisitioning of railways and other public works. After the constitutional assembly was established, the first laws passed included land reform, public health, and police system reforms. The aim of these legal measures was to establish a common set of laws and regulations to be followed throughout Poland. This was the first effort towards administrative unification after Poland's independence.

An important law passed unanimously throughout Poland was the Constitutional Act of March 17, 1921. This act constitutes the current constitution of the new Poland. It covers all issues, including the generation of legislative and political power, the provision of compulsory military service for all citizens, and the affirmation of religious freedom. In short, in a comprehensive manner, this act clearly stipulates the obligations of the people and their rights to be enjoyed.

However, the establishment of this act was not enough to eliminate the traces of more than a century of division in Poland. Since the last partition, Poland had been divided into three parts, with completely different administrative and legislative systems. The only thing that maintained the patriotic concept of Polish merchants was the Polish language used everywhere. This Poland, which had undergone prolonged analysis, also required a considerable period to achieve true and consistent unification. Even obvious matters.

Therefore, the legal systems of the previous era were still largely considered valid in both the administrative and judicial parts. This was a real situation forced by the environment, not what the legislators wanted. The legislators' goal was to make Poland a unified country implementing a local autonomy system, not a federal country in which each part governs itself.

The administrative outline of Poland is also specified in this constitution. The country is divided into sixteen provinces (Voierodie), and each province is further divided into towns (Starostie) and villages (Commune), etc. According to the principles of local decentralization and local autonomy, each district is assisted by a council elected by the people to execute administrative affairs with government officials.

Warmth in the Heart (272)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 14: Emerald Bamboo Sheds Tears, Her Heart Breaks; Red Lotus Fades, a Woman's Soul Departs

People from Ningbo also have a spirit of adventure. So in the country, no matter which place opens a new port, it is the Ningbo people who first come to engage in business. Moreover, they are devoted to their hometown ties. Fellow villagers are always willing to promote their fellow villagers. Pulling up weeds, they are naturally gradually becoming a part of the domestic power. As the saying goes (those who endure the most bitterness, rise above others.) Ningbo people are very able to embrace these two sentences. It is said that the man that Cuiyun married was also one of the Ningbo merchants. Speaking of his background, it was also very humble. But he was able to constantly struggle with difficulties. He was also able to constantly seize his opportunities without losing them. Now he has actually made himself a compradore on a Yangtze River steamer. This person's surname is Zhang, his courtesy name is Yiqing. When he married Cuiyun, he was already over forty years old. Which young women would not want to marry a young man? Why would they like someone past middle age? At that time, Cuiyun was only about twenty years old. Comparing her age with Zhang Yiqing's age, Zhang Yiqing could well be her father. How could she willingly marry him? Cuiyun at that time was a free person, not someone else's wife for sale. But she was someone who had experienced the battlefield of love. The guests who walked around in her place were not without young people. Things in the world are often not perfect. Young people are mostly frivolous and impractical. Some do not have the property rights in their hands. Some secretly come out to play, hiding it from their parents. If she were to marry that kind of youth, there would be no good results in the future. And it is close to an adventurous nature. Those girls who are brave enough to take risks do not care if he is young or old. They temporarily plan for immediate enjoyment. One side takes the initiative to extract your money. By the time everyone is tired of enjoying themselves, the money has also been squeezed dry. You go your way, I go my way. Each to the east, not related to each other. There are also those who, as mentioned earlier, have long harbored the intention of taking a bath. But Cuiyun did not think this way. She always wanted to marry a reliable person and live in peace, without wanting to leave the mountain. But from among the many young guests, she secretly chose and chose, but she was never satisfied. There was one of them. She could be very satisfied with him. But she had a heart for him, but he did not have a heart for her. This cannot be forced on people. There was also another one. She also had a heart for him. He also had a heart for her. But he already had a wife. And his wife would never allow him to marry a concubine. If Cuiyun were to focus on that guest and must marry him, it could be secretly carried out. But she knew that there could be no good results. Not only would she harm herself, but she would also harm him. At that time, Zhang Yiqing took a fancy to her. How capable he was, how extensive his social life was. Because she saw other Ningbo people, they were always rigid. But he was so considerate and gentle to her.

There are Tianjin Buyers for Guest Indica Rice

Yesterday, Guest Indica rice continued to arrive from Jiangxi, with a small amount also arriving in Shanghai from Hunan. However, Hunan has officially lifted the ban, so there may be a large number arriving continuously. After the official lifting of the ban in Hunan Province, the passport fee decreased by one yuan compared to goods shipped last month. With reduced costs, traders are naturally more interested. Therefore, the Shanghai market is very stagnant, with prices declining slightly. For the whole day, merchants from Tianjin bought 1,000 bags of Hunan Broken Rice at a price of 11 yuan 7-8 jiao. Jiangxi rice is popular among merchants on this street and sells better, so the market is stable. It is estimated that 2,000 bags of early machine rice were sold at prices of 13 yuan 4 jiao 5 fen, 13 yuan, and 12 yuan 8 jiao, and 800 bags of late machine rice were sold at prices of 14 yuan 9 jiao, 14 yuan, and 13 yuan 6 jiao.

The Flour Market Re-enters a Difficult Situation

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, the prices for each month presented another trend of gradual softening. Although the quoted price of foreign wheat rose by 4-5 jiao, actual sales were slackening. Tianjin merchants were still unable to ship exports, so the attitude of various factories was not as firm as before. Additionally, the pricing of foreign flour and wheat had become close. If the pricing of local flour was not lower than that of foreign flour, it would inevitably increase gradually. Therefore, although the factories did not sell off significantly, the future situation would ultimately be difficult to develop. As a result, this month was down by 2.5 li compared to last week, October was down by 1 fen, November was down by 5 li, December was down by 2.5 li, January was down by 2.5 li, and February was down by 5 li.

The Futures Wheat Evening Market Sees Heavy Selling and a Sudden Drop

Yesterday, after the opening of the futures wheat market in the morning, the prices for each month generally showed a hovering trend, with little increase or decrease compared to last week's closing price. However, after the opening in the afternoon, the market was initially stable. Then, a major player suddenly sold off a large quantity of distant months, such as December, January, and February, reaching 50-60 truckloads. According to general speculation, it was said to be the hedging of factories. Therefore, sentiment softened, and the market trend began to decline. Generally, the pricing of foreign wheat is approaching, so the focus of factories must change. As a result, this month was down by 3 fen compared to last week, November and December were down by 3 fen, and January and February were each down by 5 fen. In the spot wheat market, sources from the Guest route continued to arrive, but the purchasing interest of various factories remained unchanged. Given this type of firm rejection, the quoted prices for each grade must be revised downward in the future without a doubt. Yesterday, more than 1,000 bags of wheat from Tai'erzhuang, Shandong, and Yaowan were purchased by traders but have not yet been allocated to factories.

Sugar Market Japanese Sugar Arrives in Swarms, Weakening the Market

Yesterday, the report for the sugar market districts: There were no electricity reports for the current sugar from Cuba and the New York futures sugar. Java's Current Sugar price is 8.750, the future sugar for October is 8.50, and November is 8.375. This is each dropping back 125 than before. At the association marketplace, the trade for Dutch sugar No. 24 and raw white sugar still is scarce; for the moment they’re putting through the good of aged, at 8 liang. The cleanliness is white for the goods that pull thick at 8 liang 3 qian. The coming in and coming out is very lax. Transactions for medium white sand and such are also few, Dutch red, with the good arriving transferring in swarms, the market vigor is even weaker. Although there is no coming in and coming out, the shape of the market has already revealed a trend of decline, the Japanese sugar N mark is at 8 liang 1 qian 2.5 fen, YT mark is at 8 liang 0 qian 7.5 fen, YRO mark is at 7 liang 9 qian 7.5 fen, YP mark is at 8 liang 1 qian 7.5 fen each dipping back 2.5 fen, transactions are particularly withered. The actual matter is that selling is sluggish, at the Yangtze etc. the sales office of Taikoo sugar has even dropped the price half a qian. Therefore, the asking of the way is even more calm, and the Meiji sugar is continuously in transit to arrive, although the multiple families still think of tightening things, it already feels like the turning of the decadent style is difficult to avoid.

North and South Goods New Quanzhou Soaked Round Comes on Stage for This Batch

Quanzhou new soaked round goods, because the same profession has fixed a time for export, may not preempt one another. Thus they were delayed a couple of days arriving here at Shanghai and the figure has increased, a total of 3,000 plus boxes. Yesterday it has already been loaded aboard the Hua Heng ship and arrived, here at new same rounds goods have already dropped three surface values, as it happens to match the market fatigue it is difficult to hope for good selling. Inspect that this batch of high goods is valued at around 37 liang, it is bound to exhaust itself. Cover the market that this the surface value has also decreased 1 or 2 liang again.

Silk and Tea Shaoxing's New Autumn Cocoons are Already on the Market

There is an 80% Harvest Overall ··· The Price of Improved Seed Cocoons Looks High

This year, farmers in the four rural areas of Shaoxing are raising autumn silkworms because the official authorities are selling improved seeds and silk cocoon merchants are promoting and advocating it. The amount of silkworms raised is not less than that of spring silkworms. From the acquisition of silkworm eggs to the third sleep and sufficient leaves, the silkworm season has been quite good and the climate has been harmonious. But until the big sleep and abundant leaves the weather suddenly changed, autumn rains came one after another. With the added coldness, the silkworm eggs developed, changing without sleeping or eating. They suffered great losses. The new silkworms from the four rural areas are now on the market. About 50% of the cocoon businesses are weighing the goods. The yield of cocoons is about 80% of a normal year. The price of cocoons is highest for the improved varieties, with a price of 60 yuan, while ordinary varieties are priced at 40 to 50 yuan.

Piece Goods Dong Goods Skyrocket Fiercely

Locally-Made Cloth: The market has seen little prosperity or decline in recent days, but sales are not as smooth as before. The main reason is that the price of Dong piece goods has recently skyrocketed, causing the focus of local merchants to shift, leading to a large decrease in sales. However, factory stocks are very low, so no decline has yet been seen. Yesterday, Ningbo merchants slightly traded 16-pound coarse cloth, with Wang Lao priced at 7 liang 1 qian 5 fen, Double Elephant at 7 liang, and Five Cranes at 7 liang 2 qian 5 fen. Fine cloth sales are stagnant due to dyeing and sales issues, and the Northern merchants are also inactive. Yesterday, there was a slight softening, with Blue Double Fish selling for 6 liang 9 qian 5 fen, Yang Crane for 6 liang 9 qian, and Hunter for 6 liang 8 qian. Fine twill is still firm, with strong demand from inland merchants. Yang Crane sold for 7 liang 2 qian 5 fen, Golden City for 7 liang 1 qian, and Blue Double Fish for 6 liang 8 qian 2 fen.

Eastern and Western Piece Goods: Yesterday, Eastern goods rose again, with an unstoppable momentum. Fine broadcloth rose by another 2.5 to 5 li, with Lake Heart Pavilion at 2 qian 7 fen 5 li already set. Spot goods sold for 2 qian 7 fen. Zijin Mountain opened at 2 qian 6 fen 7 li 5 hao. Straight tribute satin rose by 1 fen across the board, with Five Roads requiring 3 qian 7 fen 2 li 5 hao, Eight Horses 3 qian 6 fen 7 li 5 hao, and Magpie Bridge Meeting Flying Horse Child consistently at 2 qian 8 fen 2 li 5 hao. Other items, such as cotton flannel, moon velvet, red label twill, etc., also saw firmness. Besides the exceptionally active future street, Qingdao, Xuzhou, Sichuan, and other merchants also made large purchases yesterday. Observing the follow-up steps, there is a strong trend of continued growth and increase. Western goods also rose, but the future street was not significantly different.

Hardware and Screws Local Merchants See Extremely Active Trading

The screw business has been very lively recently, with transactions reaching as many as 600-700 barrels in recent days. Exports to the Yangtze River, inland rivers, and Fujian merchants have also seen some additions. Therefore, the vibrancy of negotiations in the market is almost comparable to that of Dong white iron. The current market price is 12 liang for 3-fen screws, 11 liang 5 qian for 4-fen screws, 11 liang for 5-fen screws, and 8 liang 7 qian 5 fen for 6-fen screws. Recent arrivals have been very few, and stocks are low, so the market outlook is optimistic.

Miscellaneous Items Cement Sold for 700 Barrels

Yesterday, a construction merchant in this city purchased 700 barrels of Elephant brand cement at a price of 3 liang 7 qian 5 fen. It was handled by a hardware store on North Suzhou Road. It is said that the transaction of Elephant brand has been very lively recently, it is because the market is inexpensive,

Hu Nan

Yesterday in the Hu Nan Rice Market, the Qingjiao Gang arrived with two boats. Sales in urban and rural markets were limited. New early rice prices were down by 20 cents. Yangjian and Sanjian rice were also down by 10 cents. Only thick early rice and thin late rice increased by 20 cents. There were no goods from Changshu, Wuxi, Northern Jiangsu, or Southern Jiangsu to supply the market.
