Local News

Today's Commemoration of the Premier's First Uprising

The Municipal Executive Committee Issues a Proclamation to the People

Today is the anniversary of the first uprising of Mr. Sun Yat-sen, the Premier of the Chinese Kuomintang. The Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department has specifically scheduled a commemorative meeting to be held at 9:00 AM today at the Republican Grand Theater on Fangbang Bridge, Min'guo Road. All government agencies, party departments at all levels, and people's organizations are required to send four representatives to attend at that time. Yesterday, a proclamation to the people was also issued, saying:

British Envoy Passes Through Shanghai to Beijing

Expected to Arrive in Beijing Yesterday Afternoon

The Damei Evening News reports that the British Minister, Lampson, traveled to Beijing from Beidaihe aboard the gunboat HMS Scarab. He passed through Shanghai yesterday (the 7th), but only stopped briefly at the Wusongkou. After the British Consulate-General sent a small boat to deliver and receive correspondence, he immediately sailed west. It is expected that he will arrive in Beijing this afternoon. According to the British Consulate-General, Lampson's trip is only a routine visit to Beijing to meet and discuss official business and does not involve any special missions.

Foreign Minister Returned to Beijing Last Night

Waiting to Meet the British Envoy

Foreign Minister Tu Zhengting, who recently traveled to Hangzhou for sightseeing, returned to Shanghai by train at approximately 2:00 PM yesterday. Mr. Wang learned that the British Envoy Lampson had departed from Beidaihe on a British warship, heading south to Beijing. According to a telegram from Mr. Lampson en route, he is expected to arrive today. Mr. Wang then took the overnight express train back to Beijing last night to await a meeting with the British Envoy to negotiate the October 1st handover of Weihaiwei. Mr. Wang originally intended to host a grand tea dance at the Dahua Hotel today to welcome Mr. Roxas, the Vice Speaker of the Philippine House of Representatives, who is passing through Shanghai on the President Wilson, and personally receive him. However, due to the urgent need to meet with the British Envoy, he had to return to Beijing hastily. Mr. Wang entrusted Vice Foreign Minister Li Jinlun to chair today's tea party at Dahua. Mr. Li is expected to arrive in Shanghai from Beijing this morning.

Joint Defense of Shanghai, Songjiang, Nanhui, and Fengxian Counties

Shanghai, Songjiang, Nanhui, and Fengxian counties are implementing joint defense. A meeting was held at the Fengxian County Government on the afternoon of the 6th to discuss the implementation. Shanghai County sent Ding Ji'en to attend. Yesterday, Mr. Ding returned to Shanghai and told a Guowen News Agency reporter that the joint defense meeting was convened by Fengxian County because the military situation at the front is currently busy, and the defense of the rear is of great importance. Moreover, bandits are cunning and choose to appear and disappear at the borders of neighboring areas, making it impossible for the suppression personnel to pursue and suppress them, limited by boundaries. By the time a document is issued for encirclement and capture, the bandits have long since fled. Therefore, Shen Qingchen, the magistrate of Fengxian County, wanted to overcome this difficulty and, based on the Wudan Wucheng joint defense plan, specifically convened a meeting of the Shanghai, Songjiang, and Nanhui counties to discuss joint defense. Once a bandit alarm is encountered, regardless of jurisdictional boundaries, all efforts will be made to suppress and capture them, so the bandits will have no room to breathe, and it will be even more difficult for them to take advantage of the border areas to hide. More than 20 people attended the meeting the day before yesterday, including Liu Zhao, a representative of the First Water Police District, Shen Qingchen of Fengxian, Ding Ji'en of Shanghai, Zhang Qianshou of Songjiang, and Cai Churen of Nanhui, with Shen Qingchen presiding. Since the plan's regulations had not yet been drafted, a preparatory meeting was first held, and a formal joint defense meeting will be held after everything is ready. The resolutions of the meeting included: (1) It was resolved to name the organization the "Shanghai, Songjiang, Nanhui, and Fengxian Counties Joint Defense Committee"; (2) It was resolved that the regulations would be drafted by Fengxian and then submitted to the formal meeting; (3) It was resolved to invite the party departments of each county to participate in the name of the preparatory committee; (4) It was resolved that the monthly expenses would be set at 120 yuan; (5) It was resolved to elect Shen Qingchen, the magistrate of Fengxian County, as the director of the preparatory committee.

Changsha Market Peaceful, Telegraph

Exchange Rates Normal

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce previously telegraphed the Hankou Chamber of Commerce to inquire whether the Changsha market was peaceful. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce has now received a quick letter from the Hankou General Chamber of Commerce, stating: "We have received your telegram. After investigation, the Changsha market is peaceful, and exchange rates are normal. We are replying to your inquiry."

Chinese Yangtze Steamers

Full Resumption of Operations from Tomorrow

Chinese Steamers on the Yangtze Return to Shanghai: The communist party of Xiang province, which had committed offenses, has recently been repelled by the Xiang army, and Changsha is now secure. There is no need for the central government to dispatch large numbers of troops to Hunan. Yesterday in Beijing, after the request of China Merchants, Sanbei and others, the Ministry of Communications issued a telegraphed reply at noon, approving the return of the Jianghua, Jiangxin, Jiangda and other ships to Shanghai, in order to restore navigation on the Yangtze River. The ships are permitted to arrive in Shanghai today, and will immediately fully resume service. Since the Yangtze River route has been suspended recently, just as the ban on the export of rice from Jiangxi and Hunan has been lifted and large quantities of rice are being transported to Shanghai, foreign steamers from Britain and Japan have taken the opportunity to compete for business. Yesterday, the China Merchants Bureau received news of the return of all its Yangtze River ships. Shen Zhongyi and Li Yunliang, the chiefs of the Business Department, immediately planned the resumption of navigation on the Yangtze River. It was resolved yesterday afternoon that the Bureau's Yangtze River ships would fully resume service from the 10th, with the Jiangjing opening the first ship, still running the regular 1-4-3-6 schedule. A notice was immediately issued to all passengers and freight forwarders that the Yangtze River passenger and freight services would resume as usual from today. At the same time, a telegram was sent to the branch offices in various ports ordering them to start soliciting cargo from the 10th.

Sanbei Will Also Operate Yangtze River Steamers: The Sanbei Company, due to the gradual increase in cargo for the Yangtze River, and in order to compete with foreign merchants, has specially added the ocean liners Hengshan and Longshan to the Yangtze River route to meet the needs of passengers and merchants. Now that the Xinning Xing steamer has been released and allowed to return, it is scheduled to be dispatched on the regular route from the 10th, while the Hongyuan and Hongheng steamers will be dispatched to the upper reaches, and the Wuxing steamer has not yet been released.

Chinese Steamers to be Escorted by Troops: Along the Yangtze River, in places such as Daye and Wuxue, there are frequent incidents of attacks. The China Merchants Bureau, in order to ensure the safety of the returning Yangtze River steamers, the safety of passengers, and peace of mind, has specially requested the Capital Garrison Command to dispatch armed military police to be stationed on the ships, at least four on each ship, and steel bulletproof plates have been installed outside the driver's room.

Difficulties for Steamers to Travel to Shashi: There are many bandits lurking in the vicinity of Shashi and Hao Xue in the upper Yangtze River, and merchant ships traveling to and from the area are often fired upon. The navies of Britain and Japan have each dispatched a warship to Shashi to protect the navigation of the steamers. The Japanese residents in the area have also been transported to Hankou by Japanese warships. Yesterday, the China Merchants Bureau received a telegram from the Kuailee steamer, stating that it had arrived in Hankou from Shashi and that the journey was still safe. Also, the Bureau's Yangtze River steamer Emei, which was returning to Shanghai from Yichang, suffered damage to the wing engine and other components on the left side of the ship when it was reversing while docking in Zhenjiang. It now needs to be towed to Shanghai for major repairs.

Inspectorate General of Customs

Planning to Establish Customs Houses at Huludao and Weihaiwei

Moylerh Visits and Inspects Two Ports

And Investigates and Improves Customs Affairs at Dalian Customs

Moylerh, the Inspector General of Customs, left Shanghai on the 1st of this month aboard the Customs cruiser Hai Hsin. There were various rumors about whether he was going to Hong Kong, Andong, or Dalian. A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency went to the Inspectorate General of Customs on Hede Road yesterday to inquire and met with an official. According to him, Moylerh is going to Huludao to inspect the port and prepare for the establishment of a customs house. He will also visit Dalian to investigate customs affairs because Dalian is a special zone, and the customs treatment for goods transported there is different from that of goods transported to Tianjin and other places. There is a tax on each item, and the inspection method is also different. This trip is to investigate and improve the situation. On his way back, Moylerh will also go to Weihaiwei to inspect and prepare for the establishment of a customs house after it is recovered on October 1st. As for going to Hong Kong to meet with the Governor to discuss the establishment of a customs house in Kowloon, there was a proposal for this before the new year, but Moylerh will probably not have time to go there for a while after returning to Shanghai.

Li Zhonggong Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning

Recent News on the Jinliyuan Case

Li Zhonggong, the Vice Minister of Communications who also serves as the General Manager of the China Merchants Bureau, arrived in Shanghai from Beijing at 7:00 AM yesterday. Cai Pei, the Director of Navigation Administration who is also the General Manager of the China Merchants Bureau, went to meet him. According to Mr. Li, he will take office at the Bureau within this week. General Manager Cai has already informed all departments to prepare for the handover procedures.

According to General Manager Cai, regarding the Jinliyuan Wharf case, lawyer Gao Shuo is in daily contact with the Father of the San De Tang. The San De Tang is currently waiting for a reply telegram from the Paris headquarters. Once the reply telegram arrives, the mediation will proceed immediately. If the mediation fails, arbitration will be conducted. Currently, the Bureau is not overly disputing the San De Tang's intention to take back a portion of the warehouses on the wharf, because even if they were leased, they were always subleased and there was no profit to be made. As for the entire wharf, the San De Tang has agreed to sell or renew the lease to the Bureau.

Cheng Zhenjun Returns to China Today

Cheng Zhenjun, the Director of the Construction Department of Zhejiang Province, who was previously sent abroad for inspection, has now returned to China on the Asama Maru. He is expected to arrive at the Huishan Wharf at 10:00 AM this morning.

Records of Contemporary Figures' Movements

Niu Yongjian, the Minister of the Interior, and Liu Peiquan, the Commander of Yunnan Aviation, both went to Beijing by overnight train last night.

Zhang Jingjiang, the Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, arrived in Shanghai from Hangzhou at 10:15 AM yesterday morning.

Delegation from the National Private Electrical Industry Association Visits Shanghai

The National Private Electrical Industry Association held a meeting in Beijing to welcome Shen Sifang and others, who were representing China at the World Power Conference. In order to improve China's electrical industry, a delegation was formed to conduct a thorough on-site investigation. The delegation departed the day before yesterday, following the Beijing-Shanghai Railway line, first to Wuxi, Changzhou, Suzhou, and other places to visit electrical factories. They are scheduled to arrive in Shanghai from Suzhou this morning. After disembarking, they will first visit the Shanghai Municipal Council Electricity Department, and tomorrow they will visit the Nanshi Chinese Electrical Company and the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company. The day after tomorrow, they will take the early train to Hangzhou and other places for visits.

Naval Academy Students Scheduled to Depart for Japan

To be Escorted by Li Shijia

The students of the Naval Academy who are sent to study torpedoes and naval supply in Japan, including He Xikun, Zeng Guoshen, Yao Yu, Ye Kejue, Li Huiji, Menghan Ding, Zhang Dacheng, Chen Hong and other eight students, arrived in Shanghai from Beijing yesterday morning and stayed at the Naval Reorganization Office in Gaochang Temple. They are scheduled to set sail on the 23rd of this month, first to Tokyo. It is reported that the Navy Ministry has contacted Lieutenant General Ban Ban of the Japanese Army regarding all admission procedures, and has appointed Li Shijia, the Director of the General Affairs Department of the Navy Ministry, to escort the students to Japan when the time comes in order to arrange the details. Mr. Li is currently still in Beijing and will come to Shanghai around the 20th, and will set off for Japan together.

China Industrial and Commercial Management Association

Minutes of the Meeting of the Finance Group of the Special Committee

The China Industrial and Commercial Management Association held the second research meeting of the finance group of the special committee at the Lianhua General Association yesterday. The meeting discussed the details and methods drafted by Deputy Director Li Quanshi and Committee Member Cai Chengxin. After a detailed discussion of the research outline by the committee members, some minor revisions were made, and the following resolutions were passed: (1) Director Xu Jilin, Deputy Director Li Quanshi, and Committee Member Shen Laiqing were assigned to study the issues of issued corporate bonds and fundraising; (2) Committee Member Jin Guodou and Committee Member Cai Chengxin were assigned to study the issue of promoting the circulation of commercial paper; (3) Committee Member Shou Yicheng, Committee Member Wang Zhixin, and Committee Member Dai Ailu were assigned to study the issues of public debt funds and surplus distribution, and Xu Yongzuo and Pan Xulun were specially invited to assist in the study; (4) Committee Member Yang Dunfu and Committee Member Zhu Chengzhang were assigned to study the issue of capital utilization, and Mr. Tang Shoumin was specially appointed as a member of the group to study this issue. The revised plan is recorded below: The research scope and methods of the finance group: (1) Research scope (1) Various financial issues when establishing an enterprise: (A) Whether the predetermined capital amount is commensurate with the nature and scope of the business, and the allocation of fixed and current assets; (B) Whether the methods of raising capital are commensurate with its nature; (C) The issue of the par value of shares; (D) The issue of official interest on shares; (E) The issue of preparatory expenses; (2) Capital utilization and expansion issues after the establishment of an enterprise: (A) Utilization of capital: (i) Prior supervision; (ii) Contemporary supervision; (iii) Subsequent supervision; (B) Methods of capital expansion: (i) Increasing shares, bonus shares, and others; (ii) Raising corporate bonds; (iii) Public accumulation; (C) Distribution of surplus (Conflict between the overall interests of the enterprise and the individual interests of shareholders); (3) Liquidation and merger of enterprises; 2. Research methods: (A) Case study; (B) Problem study;

Ministry of Industry and Commerce

Correcting the Habit of Liquidating Shops

Must Use the Name of Liquidation According to Law

Procedures Must Follow Legal Regulations

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce recently stated that the bankruptcy of industrial and commercial enterprises often uses the name of liquidation to dispose of assets freely, disregarding the law, harming society, and having a significant impact. In fact, the law only provides for liquidation, not the name of liquidation, and the procedures are often non-compliant. Previously, the Shanghai Certified Public Accountants Association requested a general order to correct the situation, which has been approved. A general order will be issued to the whole country. In the future, if shops go bankrupt, they must comply with the Civil Code and the Company Law, change to liquidation, and handle matters according to law. The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, after receiving the request from the Association, has also instructed the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to inform the industry associations and notify the industrial and commercial sectors to pay attention. The approval order from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce is recorded below: (Order No. 12484 of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce) The original submission was made by the Shanghai Certified Public Accountants Association, stating that recent liquidation cases are accustomed to customs, not fully legal, and have a huge impact on society. Please approve a general order to correct the name and authority. Upon review, regarding liquidation matters, when the general liquidation of the Civil Code is conducted, it should be handled in accordance with the law, and the terms liquidation and liquidator should be used to comply with the regulations. In addition to a general order, you are hereby notified. This is the approval order.

Cease Issuing Rewards to Wounded Soldiers

The Municipal Government Ordered to Comply

The Xin Shanghai News Agency reports that the Shanghai Municipal Government yesterday received an order from the Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, stating that in the future, the issuance of rewards and allowances to wounded soldiers should be stopped in order to avoid fostering the bad habit of laziness among wounded soldiers. In addition, wounded and sick soldiers in hospitals must be strictly supervised to maintain local security. The Municipal Government has approved the consultation and has sent letters to various legal organizations and agencies to comply.

Military Department Strictly Investigates the Private Transportation of Saltpeter and Sulfur

The Shipping Association yesterday received a ban from the Ministry of Communications, forwarded by the Ministry of Military Administration, ordering all shipping companies to comply. The original letter stated: "The Ministry of Communications issued Order No. 2620, stating that saltpeter and sulfur are raw materials for the manufacture of military fire, and private transportation and trafficking have long been strictly prohibited. The application for merchant transportation should also be strictly limited. Now that the communist bandits in various provinces are taking the opportunity to commit crimes, the origin of these raw materials should be thoroughly investigated and strictly examined to prevent malpractices and curb the spread of unrest. In the future, when companies, factories, and businesses in various places purchase and transport saltpeter and sulfur and submit applications through your Ministry to apply for saltpeter and sulfur passports, in addition to verifying whether the statutory procedures are complied with, the purpose, type, and quantity should also be carefully reviewed and then forwarded for application. Those transported from commercial ports to the interior must be reviewed and forwarded by the local government or provide equivalent proof before being allowed to be transported. In addition to separate consultations, you are requested to investigate and handle the matter accordingly." Private transportation of saltpeter and sulfur has long been prohibited. In the future, when ships transport saltpeter and sulfur, they must verify whether there is a passport or equivalent proof before they can be transported. In addition to separate distribution, you are hereby ordered to have the Association inform all shipping companies to comply and report on the compliance situation. This is the order." The Association has urgently forwarded the letter and requests that you investigate and handle the matter accordingly.

Appeal of the Vendors in the French Concession

Over a Thousand Vendors Suddenly Unemployed

The Vendors Association Petitions the French Authorities for Relief

On the sidewalks of the French Concession's Minquan Road and Avenue du Roi Albert and other areas, there have always been vendor stalls. Recently, the French police, in view of the fact that a small number of vendors were not setting up stalls in accordance with the police regulations, and for the sake of facilitating traffic, strictly prohibited all vendors, regardless of size, from setting up any stalls. The vendors, fearing the loss of their livelihoods and impending death, unanimously requested the French Concession Vendors Association to find ways to maintain their livelihoods. Yesterday, the association submitted a petition to the French Concession authorities requesting relief. The original petition stated: "According to the more than one thousand vendor households of our association, and the hundred or so representatives, who reside on Minquan Road, Rue Min Tche Ni Yin, Avenue du Roi Albert, Avenue Foch, Avenue Petain, and Avenue Mareschal Joffre, and other areas under your jurisdiction, they declared that since each vendor household obtained a permit to set up a stall and conduct business in those areas, they have done so for many years. The location of their stalls has never obstructed traffic or the business of shops, and thus no accidents have occurred to date. However, recently, the French police, for unknown reasons, have suddenly expelled all vendors from the areas in question, a total of more than one thousand vendor households of all sizes, and prohibited them from setting up stalls. As a result, more than one thousand vendor households, with a total of seven thousand men, women, and children, are suddenly without food and are now crying out in hunger, on the verge of starvation. They have no avenue for appeal and can only implore our association to find ways to maintain their livelihoods and save their lives. In response, we have investigated and found that the stalls set up on the sidewalks of each road all have permits. Although there may be a small number of vendors whose stalls are too large and should be prohibited, the majority of stalls comply with the order. Now, all vendors in the areas in question are being prohibited indiscriminately, not only causing more than one thousand vendors to suddenly lose their jobs, but also causing their families, who depend entirely on their livelihoods, to starve. Moreover, the impact on local security is significant. Our association, in order to seek a livelihood for the vendors and to seek peace for the locality, proposes that vendors be allowed to set up stalls in places that do not affect local traffic. We should also set appropriate rules so that each vendor can abide by the order and engage in business with peace of mind. In this way, several members of a family can live at the same time, and the local security will also benefit. Now, we are submitting the various stall setting rules that our association has formulated on separate paper. We ask whether they are feasible, and we sincerely hope that you will examine them and approve them for the sake of public convenience. Respectfully submitted to the French Consul General in Shanghai, Gan; the Director of the French Municipal Council, Wei; and the Director of the French General Police Station, Fei. Shanghai French Concession Vendors Association, September 8th, year 19 of the Republic of China."

Municipal Land Bureau

Surveying Land in the Yinxiang District

Twenty-three Baozheng and Nineteen Tu

The Municipal Land Bureau issued a notice yesterday stating: "Notice: The bureau is now beginning to survey the land of the Yinxiang District's twenty-three baozheng and nineteen tu. All property owners should pay attention to the following: (1) The dibao (local security) will distribute registration forms to the property owners. All property owners should fill them out truthfully within ten days of receiving the form and have the dibao collect them and submit them to the third surveying team of the bureau, or the property owners can submit them directly to the surveying team. (2) If the property owner's address is unknown, making it impossible to distribute the registration form, they can directly submit the form to the bureau or the third surveying team themselves. (3) If the property owner's title deeds are mortgaged and unavailable, making it impossible to fill in the title deed's household name and mu (unit of area), they should quickly copy them from the mortgagee and must not refuse. (4) When the land of each household is being surveyed, the property owner must, together with the dibao, clearly point out the boundaries to the investigator or surveyor, or delegate a representative to the site to point out the boundaries in advance. Otherwise, the bureau will only rely on the dibao's instructions, and the property owner will be responsible for any errors or disputes that may arise in the future. The above four items are related to the property owner's consolidation of property rights and should be given special attention. This notice."

Recent Tragic Disaster in Ankang, Shaanxi

The Chinese Relief Society has received reports from Zhang Xiaoci, president of the Ankang Huayang Relief Association in the old Hanzhong Road of Shaanxi, and Xia Minghua, vice president, stating that Ankang has suffered from drought since the great drought of the Republic of China 14th year, followed by locust plagues. There has been drought every year, and nine out of ten households are empty. Harvests are meager, and people are displaced by famine. Bandits gather and cause trouble, and banditry and kidnapping are increasing day by day. Those who could provide relief in the past are now unable to save themselves. The disaster victims are now without a way out. In October of last year and March of this year, there were two attacks on the city, and the residents were reduced to ruins. Since May 7th, the city has been besieged again. The siege lasted two months until July 7th, when relief troops broke the siege. The economy was in panic, and food supplies were cut off. The price of a dou (unit of volume) of wheat was 12 yuan, and the price of a dou of rice was 24 yuan. Wheat flour was 0.3 yuan per jin (unit of weight). Prices were so expensive, and there was no place to buy them. People dug for mice and exchanged children and dissected bones. The suffering is unbearable. Our association took the opportunity to provide emergency relief and raised more than 2,500 yuan to distribute for relief. It was a drop in the bucket and did not help much. The old and weak fled, and thousands left the city every day, but they were unable to escape because of the thorny roads and were often robbed. There were more than 3,200 households affected. This year's wheat harvest was expected, but it was trampled and destroyed before it matured. Troops were stationed on all sides, and conscriptions and levies forced people to sell their daughters and children. It was impossible to provide for them. A survey of the disaster victims showed that there were approximately 46,500 people. Those who have not been surveyed cannot be counted. Compared with the great drought three years ago and the siege of the provincial capital in the 15th year, the suffering has increased several times. Please provide a large sum of money to relieve the suffering and save lives. We have already allocated 30,000 bottles of relief medicine, Jisheng Dan, to be shipped to Tianjin and then allocated to the various disaster areas for distribution to temporarily relieve the urgent needs. We hope that people of goodwill in the country will work together to save the situation in order to alleviate the catastrophe and invoke the harmony of heaven."

Local News 2

A Big Gunfight With Thieves on Rue Sapey Yesterday Afternoon

Detectives Hear of Robbery and Go to Arrest

Both Sides Exchange More Than Ten Shots

No One Was Injured

Three Robbers Were Arrested on the Spot

At around 11:00 AM yesterday, six robbers suddenly arrived at the home of Cheng Luan, a Hunanese who had previously held an important position in the Northern military and political circles, at 308 Rue Sapey in the French Concession. On the pretext of asking questions, they rushed in through the back door. Each robber was armed with a pistol. Two robbers stood guard downstairs, tying up all the people in the house with hemp ropes and locking them in a room. The other four robbers went upstairs to rummage through boxes and chests, looting almost everything. They stole a gold watch worth 100 yuan, 30 yuan in banknotes, and 10 yuan in cash. The robbers, seeing that the loot was meager and not satisfying their desires, were preparing to loot again when the doorman at 1590, a nearby number, noticed and immediately ran out to inform the Chinese patrol officer on duty at post 358 at the intersection. The patrol officer immediately used a nearby telephone to urgently report to the Rue Lokawei station. Detective Barty, the leader of the robbery squad, happened to be at the station and immediately led Chinese and foreign detectives, including the police chief, Paul, the Chinese inspector, Kim Ku-lin, detective Li Yao-long, and the detective team, all fully armed, to the scene in cars. Detective Barty first ordered the front and back of the house at 308 to be surrounded. When he saw that the front and back doors were tightly closed, he sent a Chinese patrol officer to bravely climb over the wall to coordinate with the inside. The detectives rushed in together. At that time, the robbers knew that the detectives had gathered outside the door and desperately fled over the roofs toward the sun deck. The detectives saw this and drew their guns and fired, and the robbers also opened fire to resist arrest. The two sides exchanged more than ten shots, but no one was injured. The three robbers were captured on the spot, and three pistols were seized and taken to the station. After a preliminary interrogation by the police chief, the victim's 28-year-old daughter, Cheng Xihua, was ordered to appear and testify about the robbery. She said that her father was currently in the north and did not want to report any losses in order to avoid worrying her father and being targeted by the bandits. However, the police station believed that since such a case had occurred within the concession, it should be thoroughly investigated and should not be handled casually.

The Mitsui Sues Tongsheng Case

The Problem of Promissory Note Customs

Money Shops' Custom is Ten Days

Promissory Notes Should Be Verified Immediately Upon Receipt

Yesterday's Court Session Continued Interrogation

The Point of Contention Between the Two Parties Lies Here

Following the absconding of Ho Gengxing, the comprador of the Japanese Mitsui & Co., with misappropriated funds, the Tongsheng Money Shop, in which he held shares, immediately went bankrupt. However, Mitsui held Tongsheng Shop promissory notes worth 147,429 taels of silver, which Ho had used to pay for goods. Because the shop refused to honor these notes, Mitsui shareholders, including the Japanese Mitsui Yoshinosuke, hired lawyers Li Zuyu and Okamoto to sue Tongsheng's shareholders Yao Weiyong, Zhang Xingchu, Hong Cangting, Ho Gengxing, and the manager Zhang Chunlai, demanding full repayment and legal fees. The case has been repeatedly heard by the civil court president Ying Shi of the Special District Court and reported in the newspapers. Yesterday morning, the hearing continued. Chen Tingrui, the lawyer for the defendants Yao Weiyong and others, raised objections to the phrase "Mitsui Yoshinosuke et al." in the plaintiff's statement. After a brief exchange with lawyer Li, Li presented the company's shareholder register as proof. Chen then presented his opinion on the defendants' reasons for defense, stating that the defendants' defense rested on two points: (1) that the plaintiff obtained the promissory notes in bad faith, as Zhang Chunlai's lawyer claimed that Ho Gengxing had threatened to withdraw his shares, leaving Zhang Chunlai no choice but to issue the notes. However, this does not constitute illegal extortion. (2) Assuming Ho did obtain the notes illegally, the plaintiff was a holder in good faith. Now that the defendant claims that the plaintiff was a holder in bad faith, the defendant must provide evidence to prove it. The defendant's reasons for claiming the plaintiff was a holder in bad faith are: (1) that it is customary in the money shop business for promissory notes to have a term of ten days, whereas the promissory notes in question have a term of thirty days; (2) that a foreign firm receiving promissory notes in payment for goods must only accept those issued by money shops that are members of the Money Shop Association, and Tongsheng was not a member; and (3) that upon receipt of a promissory note, the recipient should verify it with the issuing money shop, which the plaintiff failed to do. However, none of these three points is sufficient to counter the claim. Lawyer Chen argued that Li's statement had already entered the realm of debate, but that the hearing was still investigating the facts, and therefore requested that the judge allow the defendant to present the facts first, in accordance with the case procedure. The presiding judge agreed. Chen lawyer then stated that the 30-day term of the promissory notes was rarely seen, and that the dates on the notes had been altered. "My law firm represents four defendants in this case and requests that the complaint against my clients be dismissed, because my clients cannot be held responsible for the accusations. The promissory notes violate customary practice. My law firm has sent letters to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Money Shop Association for investigation. According to Article 20, Item A of the Money Shop Business Association rules, promissory notes do not have terms longer than ten days. Furthermore, Tongsheng is a non-member money shop, and the plaintiff should not have accepted the notes based on custom. Having accepted them, the plaintiff failed to investigate their origin in detail. Therefore, the plaintiff not only obtained them in bad faith, but also showed gross negligence. What warrants further investigation is that the plaintiff also admits that the promissory notes were issued through collusion between Ho Gengxing and Zhang Chunlai. Since there was such conduct, it should be invalid. Zhang Chunlai had no right to issue the notes, yet he acted beyond his authority. How can my clients be held responsible?" Subsequently, Zhang Chunlai's lawyer argued that the plaintiff was seeking a judgment ordering Zhang Chunlai to be jointly and severally liable for repayment, but Zhang only served as the shop's manager and is not legally liable for joint and several repayment, especially since he was forced to issue them by Ho, and so on. Lawyer Li briefly responded to the issue of Zhang's responsibility, but the court ordered that this point be addressed during the debate. Then, Hong Cangting's lawyer rose and stated that since Tongsheng was a partnership business, partnership assets should be liquidated first to satisfy the debts. Only if that is insufficient can a claim be made against the partners. Now, the plaintiff ignores the former and only focuses on the latter, which is not in accordance with the law, and so on. Finally, the court asked Ho Gengxing's representing lawyer Wang Youling for his opinion. The lawyer said that Ho had obtained the promissory notes from Tongsheng and transferred them to Mitsui, which was a fact, so Ho's position in the case was special. Other than this point, he would only answer questions if asked, as he was hesitant to speak for fear of showing favoritism. As for the court's question of whether Ho Gengxing had forced Zhang Chunlai to obtain the promissory notes, he had inquired with Ho Gengxing, who said that it was absolutely not the case, and so on. Lawyer Li then presented previous Tongsheng promissory notes that Ho Gengxing had given to the plaintiff, stating that the dates of redemption were all longer than ten days, so the defendant's claim that there was no such custom was not credible. The two sides debated until after noon, and the court adjourned the hearing to a later date.

University Student Involved in Lawsuit

Qiu Ruiqu Sues Fellow Villager Qiu Tiansong

For Repeatedly Insulting and Threatening Him in Writing

The Judge Urged the Defendant to Apologize and Reconcile

Qiu Ruiqu, a student in the Law School of Soochow University and a native of Fujian, has recently been subjected to insults and defamation by Qiu Tiansong (a student at Jinan University in Zhenru and an athlete), who is from the same village and shares the same surname but not the same lineage. Qiu Ruiqu was deeply resentful and hired lawyer Ma Junshuo to draft a complaint to the criminal court of the District Court, stating that the defendant Qiu Tiansong had fabricated malicious libel and threatened his life, and requesting that he be immediately arrested and severely punished to alleviate the urgent situation. The plaintiff is currently studying at the Law School of Soochow University in this city, and has always cultivated virtue and studied diligently, and has always been modest in his interactions with friends, with no prior conflicts. Unexpectedly, Qiu Tiansong, a native of the same village, has a fierce appearance and a vicious nature, and has fabricated facts, falsely claiming that the plaintiff is a lowly rabbit (i.e., a male prostitute). At first, he verbally insulted him, then he defamed him in letters, and finally, to facilitate publicity, he used postal postcards in succession, sending them like snowflakes. The postcards were clearly addressed to "Qiu Ruiqu, Rabbit (recipient)," and were filled with vulgar and obscene language that was unbearable to read, even threatening his life and intimidating him at will. One letter contained seven instances of "I will kill you" and "If I don't carry out my words, I'm not human," etc., which shows the defendant's malicious intentions and firm resolve. (Evidence includes seven letters from the defendant, before and after.) A letter of warning was sent through a lawyer and the defendant was turned over to the police station, but to no avail. In order to avoid danger, the plaintiff temporarily resided in Jiading during the summer vacation, but the defendant was well-informed and sent threatening letters again. In this situation, the defendant will not rest until he has killed the plaintiff. Furthermore, since the plaintiff was defamed by the defendant, he has been despised by teachers and friends on the one hand, and condemned by his family on the other, and has been deprived of his right to study. In fact, his reputation has been completely lost in school, at home, and in society, and his personality has been swept away. The damage is beyond words. Even if the plaintiff is lucky enough not to be killed by the defendant, what good is it to live shamelessly? The defendant's actions constitute the crimes of Article 319 and Article 325, Section 2 of the Criminal Law. In addition to seeking compensation for losses, the plaintiff hereby files a lawsuit in accordance with Article 337 of the Criminal Procedure Law, requesting that the defendant be arrested and punished according to law, and that the entire judgment be published in the newspaper to warn against unlawful behavior, etc. Yesterday morning at 10:00 a.m., Judge Deng specially opened the Third Tribunal for the trial. First, the plaintiff Qiu Ruiqu testified that he was 25 years old, a native of Fujian, and currently a third-year student at the Law School of Soochow University. He is now being harmed by the defendant's interference with his freedom and defamation of his reputation, and demands severe punishment according to the law. (Question) Have you and the defendant always been on good terms? (Answer) We are from the same village and studying together, and there is no ill will between us. (Question) There must be some reason why he wrote you insulting letters. (Answer) He was ill and asked me to go to the doctor with him, but I refused, perhaps because he harbored resentment. Also, the Fujian school sent a reward of 400 yuan to the plaintiff, which was sent to the defendant to be forwarded to the plaintiff, but the defendant did not hand over the money. The plaintiff asked him to return the money, and the defendant said that the money had been returned to Fujian. The judge, upon hearing the testimony, instructed the plaintiff: "You are both university students, and very respectable. Even if you insist on having the defendant criminally punished, it will not be good for you. Moreover, you are both from the same village, and it would be best if he could repent and not be too demanding." The plaintiff listened and said, "Yes, yes." The judge ordered the defendant Qiu Tiansong to be brought before the court. (Question) Did you write these seven letters? (Answer) Yes. The judge said: "You have committed two crimes, one of intimidation and the other of defamation. According to the law, you should be severely punished. It is best to apologize and reconcile now." The judge asked the plaintiff's lawyer if he had any opinions. Lawyer Ma stood up and said: "Both the plaintiff and the defendant in this case are university students, and this lawyer is also willing to reconcile, but there are three conditions: (1) publish an apology in the newspaper; (2) do not harass or intimidate him in the future; and (3) the money sent from Fujian (400 yuan) should be handed over by the defendant in full," etc. The judge then said to the defendant: "You have three days to reconcile at Lawyer Ma's office. If the reconciliation fails, then another hearing will be scheduled and a judgment will be made according to law." The defendant complied with the order and then the court adjourned.

Zhu Ruchao Commits Suicide and Dies From Severe Wounds

The Special District Court Verified It Yesterday

Following the arrival in Shanghai of a large sum of money sent by the Zhejiang Local Bank in Hangzhou, it was stolen for 100,000 yuan. The police have arrested a number of robbers. Zhu Ruchao, the bank's cashier among those escorting the money, had to appear in court to testify during the trial, so he stayed at the Donglai Bank. Suddenly, the day before yesterday, he committed suicide with a knife without telling anyone. The incident was reported in this newspaper, as he had been sent to the hospital for treatment. However, Zhu's injuries were fatal, and the doctors were unable to help him. He died in the hospital at midnight that evening. Upon receiving the report, the police ordered detectives to take the body to the Philand Road mortuary for verification. Donglai Bank also telegraphed Zhu Xiong San, the son of the deceased, in Hangzhou to come to Shanghai. Yesterday morning, the Special District Court commissioned Prosecutor Xu to go to the mortuary to verify that he had indeed died by suicide. After a brief inquiry, he ordered Zhu Xiong San to claim the body for coffin and burial. It is said that Zhu, in addition to asking the bank for compensation, also requested a position so as to provide for the family's livelihood. The bank has agreed to provide generous compensation, but a decision has not yet been made on whether to provide a position in the bank.

The Cai Yunhai Case Awaits Investigation Before Further Review

Cai Yunhai, a native of Guangdong, established the Cai Chen Company at the intersection of Beijing Road and Museum Road, specializing in import and export. However, those who ordered goods from him repeatedly failed to deliver the goods as scheduled after receiving the deposit and signing the contract. He has already been sued twice. This time, Guo, who ordered goods from him, sued him to the Special District Court. After investigation, it was found that he had breached the contract and failed to return the money, so he was ordered to be detained in the civil detention center. Unexpectedly, late on the night of the third of this month, Cai took advantage of a slight lapse by the guards and damaged one of the iron bars on the window of the detention center and escaped. The next day, Chinese and Western newspapers reported the incident in detail. After escaping, Cai saw the news that the court had informed the police to investigate and arrest him as soon as possible. Realizing that it would be difficult to escape the law, he hired a lawyer and surrendered himself to the Procuratorate of the Special District Court. The prosecutor specially opened an investigation court on the afternoon of the sixth, and Xie, the director of the detention center, sent Chen Jingcheng, a Shaoxing native who guarded Cai's room, to the Procuratorate for investigation. Originally, Cai wanted to be detained, but his lawyer repeatedly requested bail, so Cai was allowed to be released on bail of 500 yuan pending trial. Now that Cai has been brought to justice, the police filed a public prosecution yesterday morning, listing Cai as the first defendant, and Chen Jingcheng and Su Yunshan as the second and third defendants. Su and Chen were both guards at the detention center, so they were jointly accused. Judge Wu Tingqi reviewed the case file and learned that Cai and Chen were both under investigation in the Procuratorate. In the future, if the investigation is completed and the crime is established, the Procuratorate will definitely file a public prosecution. If the police file a lawsuit now, it seems redundant, so he ordered the three defendants, Cai Yunhai, etc., to be sent to the Procuratorate for review.

The Yu Mingrui Case

The Extortion Gang Was Interrogated Yesterday

The Gang Claims Yu's Uncle and Nephew Are Related

Yu Mingrui, a cotton yarn merchant, lives in the French Concession and is quite wealthy, which has attracted the attention of gangsters. Since this spring, he has been repeatedly threatened by extortionists. Zhang Ruigen alone has sent several extortion letters, five in total, but he is still insatiable. At 7:00 p.m. the night before last, he asked Yu to go to the Unity Hotel on Avenue Edward VII to pay the extorted money. Yu reported it to the Criminal Investigation Department of the General Police Headquarters, which dispatched detectives Pang Ruiqing and others. Yu also sent someone to the room, and just as he was negotiating with Zhang in the room, Detective Pang burst into the room and arrested Zhang. Wang Yaokun and Hua Haoquan were arrested outside the room and taken to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Special District Court, where Judge Wu interrogated them. First, Wang Yaotang, the police lawyer, presented the indictment, presenting five letters and a receipt issued by the gang as evidence. Zhang did not deny anything and confessed everything, saying that of the five letters he sent to Yu, two were written by Yu's nephew Yu Xizhang, and the other three were written by him personally. As for the 200 yuan Yu sent, he only received 170 yuan after paying 30 yuan to the person who delivered the money. The 50 yuan from another time was entirely used by Yu's uncle, and so on. The court interrogated the two defendants Wang and Hua, who both claimed that they were arrested because they went to the hotel to visit friends and did not know Zhang. Zhang also insisted that Wang and Hua were not accomplices and that he had never met them before and could not falsely accuse them. Judge Wu then ordered the defendants to be returned to custody and adjourned the hearing to a later date.

Report of Bureau Chief's Kidnapping is False

For the past two days, alarming and unfounded rumors have suddenly emerged in the Chinese areas of Nanshi, all claiming that a certain bureau chief who held an important position in public security in this city was kidnapped on his way home. The rumors spread through the streets and alleys, causing fear and suspicion among women and children. Upon hearing of this news, the reporter knew that villains were spreading rumors to create chaos and disrupt people's hearts. Out of caution, the reporter personally visited the bureau yesterday afternoon. At the time, the bureau chief was meeting with guests, so the reporter waited in the reception room. The reporter personally saw the bureau chief chatting happily with two guests, his expression vibrant and his voice loud. The reporter pondered for a long time, originally intending to meet with the bureau chief and inform him of the situation, but feared that the bureau chief would be displeased upon hearing the news, so he left without saying goodbye. However, the reporter suspects that the rumors originated from the recent martial law imposed for the 9/7 anniversary. However, if the rumors are ignored, they will spread and confuse people's hearts and cause misunderstandings. Therefore, this article is written to refute them.

Caojiadu Wujiaochang

Post Office Adds Branch

Recently, the Shanghai Postal Administration has found that the number of postal packages and items arriving from Hangzhou at the Fanhuangdu Station in western Shanghai, and the number of packages from the Zhoujiaqiao Parcel Tax Bureau, have been increasing daily, making all procedures particularly busy. To facilitate operations, it has been decided to establish another branch office in the newly built house at Wujiaochang in Caojiadu. Preparations have already begun, and the branch office will be established as soon as the construction of the house is completed at the end of this month. The existing postal branch office in the Triangle Field of the town will not be canceled for the time being.

Wusong Water Police Captain

Honored For Rescuing Abducted Victims From Danger

Gong Mianqin, the captain of the 17th Team of the 4th District of the Wusong Water Provincial Public Security Team, personally commanded the entire team of patrol boats on a flat-bottomed warship at the end of last month, heading to the Da'an Port waters at the junction of Nantong and Haimen counties outside the mouth of Wusong to suppress pirates. They intercepted a pig boat that had been robbed by pirates and rescued three abducted victims from danger. The details were reported in this newspaper. It is now known that the rescued victims Liu Fubao, Sun Yuanji, and Zhu Zugen, etc., believe that Captain Gong has made every effort to protect shipping merchants with his strict supervision of the team, and that he has personally braved gunfire and risked his life to rescue them from the pirate den, preserving their lives. They were extremely grateful and specially made a silver shield with the words "Universal Love and Support" inscribed on it. Record of the Chinese Team Banquet of the Merchant Corps

Celebrating the Award of the Shield

The Chinese team of the Shanghai International Merchant Corps celebrated its recent victory in the All-Corps Proficiency Shield competition with a banquet at the Duyichu restaurant last night. Most of the team members arrived with their families at 7:00 p.m. that afternoon, creating a lively scene with flowing skirts, clattering shoes, fragrant clothing, and gleaming hairpins. The team leader Wang Yanjing delivered a speech, followed by a speech from Hu Yunqiu, the Chinese advisor to the Corps, and a welcoming speech from the deputy team leader Chen Shixia, accompanied by the entertainment of a makeshift stage performance and a spirit group. The registered speeches of each person are recorded below.

Team Leader Wang's Speech: "The Chinese team has been established for 25 years. During these 25 years, it has undergone the arduous management and spiritual struggle of both old and new comrades, resulting in today's glory. Remembering the source of the water we drink, the reason why our Chinese team is valued by society and praised by both Chinese and Westerners is due to the tireless efforts and hard work of old and new comrades. The combination of a group must first be inspired by spirit. With sufficient spirit, there will be a strong combination and considerable achievements. The Chinese team is a security corps for merchants and civilians, and also an armed corps with a complete army system. In terms of military appearance, discipline, and cooperative spirit, it is especially important to be organized and complete. Obedience to all orders is a matter of course. Since we have taken the protection of merchants and civilians as our duty, we should serve the society. Therefore, apart from defending and protecting, there is no such thing as being responsible. Comrades, strive to continue your efforts and move forward. Finally, the award of this shield is due to the efforts of all comrades, so there will be a third victory, and we hope for a fourth, a fifth, and so on without end."

Advisor Hu's Speech: "It has been six years since the Proficiency Shield left the Chinese team. Since 1922, our team has won this shield. In 1923, we continued to win it. In 1924, the Chinese team should have won it again, but the headquarters cancelled the national encampment training due to a lack of classes, so it was cancelled in name only. Afterwards, other teams won it several times. Now, we have won first place over all the corps, winning it for the third time. Is this not due to the efforts of all of you? Because you have always been united and worked together, you have achieved such good results. As the saying goes, 'Where there is a will, there is a way.' What is especially commendable is that the members of our team are all merchants and civilians by nature, and we have always gone our own way without being tainted by political colors. Because of this, the Chinese team has been bright and shining, standing firm for 25 years as if it were just one day. I have seen other corps collapse because they were involved in political change, and some have borrowed the weight of politics to increase their own position, only to fall into a slump. As for the relationship between the merchant corps and the international community, I have never recklessly talked about politics with Westerners. If I were to talk about it, it would involve our country's politics and only invite ridicule. The fact that the politics of China are bad is not only ridiculed by foreigners, but also a disgrace to the nation. But Westerners often say that while Chinese politics are indeed bad, the Chinese team run by merchants stands out and is a model for civil corps and a credit to the international community. This is not me praising the Chinese team, but rather speaking from the perspective of Westerners. Alas, since we cannot obtain adequate protection from the government, we must gain our own strength to defend ourselves. Therefore, I have always believed that to defend ourselves, we must promote civil corps. While the Chinese team may not be said to be the first advocate of a model civil corps, it may be said to have the characteristics of a general organization, judging from its past performance. Furthermore, in terms of the current trend, it is necessary to promote sports. While good politics are like those of European and American countries, they still promote sports, and some have even raised their international status through their sporting achievements. Therefore, if our country wants to increase its international status, it has no choice but to promote sports. Our team uses shooting as a sport, and shooting is indeed superior to ball sports. It is a pity that we often do not pay attention to shooting. We know that shooting is a foreign sport. If we do not do it, then how could we have obtained today's silver shield? Now that we have obtained it, we want to keep it permanently in our team and not let it be taken away by other teams. But why did this shield that was taken from our team by other teams get taken back to our team, all of you should know that the other teams have more people with a heart to rely on others and fewer people with a sense of responsibility. There are many cases of failure due to a heavy heart to rely on others. Reflecting on our own team members, if there is anyone with a heart to rely on others, they should use the other teams as a lesson. You must also ask yourselves whether I have contributed to the success of this shield. If you feel ashamed, you must encourage yourselves to avoid repeating the same mistakes in the future. I also hope that your wives will encourage you to do so. Finally, I am very happy to see the event flourishing and should take a drink to congratulate you and wish the Chinese team unlimited future achievements." Upon finishing his speech, everyone applauded in unison.

Deputy Team Leader Chen's Welcoming Speech: "Our team has won the All-Corps Proficiency Shield and is hosting a banquet to celebrate and welcome the reappointment of Team Leader Wang. I am extremely delighted and honored. The speeches of Team Leader Wang and Advisor Hu were like setting off firecrackers, and after the firecrackers, comes my small firecracker. But as for me, I have immense happiness and a warm welcome for the reappointment of Team Leader Wang, but in terms of welcome, there are many different points. For example, the society's welcome to the officials taking office, the chief of the bureau, the president taking over, etc., this kind of welcome does not go beyond the routine, following the trend, vanity, flattery and so on. Today, my welcome to Team Leader Wang has none of the above-mentioned qualities, but there is a deeper expression, because all of us are united for the sake of peace in society, there is no involvement of rights, and there is no existence of vanity. We are not afraid of sacrificing our lives, fighting spiritually, and losing material money. There is no need to calculate because of this, and today we welcome Team Leader Wang, which is not the same as various welcomes in society, and has the utmost sincerity of the unanimous welcome of the whole team. As for the Proficiency Shield, a while ago Mr. Hu has described it in detail. I will not repeat it. It is not easy to get this shield, so we must take care to keep it, so that it can stay with our team every year and there can be today's celebration every year. This is what I deeply hope from all of you." Finally, Hao Boyang, the shooting leader, led everyone in shouting, "Long live the Chinese team, long live all comrades, long live the proficiency shield," and wished Mr. Xu Tonggu, who had worked hard and made great contributions in founding the Chinese team, a long life. For a time, cheers roared and everyone was joyful. It was truly a grand occasion. It wasn't until about 11:00 that everyone dispersed, having enjoyed themselves to the fullest.

Two Sailing Boats Collide at Wusong Estuary

Salt Boat Sinks

Sand Boat Damaged

Liu Shenglai, a fisherman from Daishan, loaded hundreds of bags of official salt at the Daishan factory to bring to Shanghai. On the early morning of the day before yesterday, he sailed to the Sanxia waters off the Wusong estuary when suddenly a large sand boat loaded with sand and mud sailed in from the outer ocean. Due to the slight fog, the two sides were unable to avoid each other, resulting in a collision. With a loud bang, the fishing boat was damaged in the middle and gradually sank. All the official salt loaded on board was soaked by the tide, causing great loss. He quickly sailed the boat close to the beach, unloaded the remaining salt, and hired another boat to transport it to Shanghai for delivery. The bow of the sand boat was also damaged, but not seriously, so it was still able to sail.

Huang Rongsheng, an apprentice at the Gaodeji board box shop on Zhongshan Road, Zhabei, was a native of Jiangwan and about 15 or 16 years old. Was the Woman's Death Due to a Buttock Injury?

Aftermath of a Verbal Dispute

Request to the Court for an Autopsy

Zhang Yingkui, a farmer from Zhangjiazhai in the Yangjing district of Pudong, had a verbal quarrel with Wang Huangshi, the wife of his neighbor Wang Nengxin, on April 29th of this year (lunar calendar), over a minor matter. Ms. Wang was pushed down by Zhang, and unfortunately, there was a farming rake on the ground. When she fell, her buttock landed on the rake, causing a wound. The police were notified, and Zhang was taken into custody by the local court. The court sentenced Zhang to 30 days of detention for negligent injury, but considering the circumstances, the sentence was suspended for two years, and he was released on bail. More than three months have passed since then, but Ms. Wang Huangshi's buttock wound has not healed. Therefore, Wang Nengxin hired a lawyer to sue in court, seeking compensation of over one hundred yuan for damages. The hearing was scheduled for yesterday. Unexpectedly, Ms. Wang Huangshi died on the 6th of this month. Wang believes that his wife's death was undoubtedly caused by the injury. Therefore, he placed the corpse in front of Zhang's house, intending to report it to the authorities. However, Zhang argued that a buttock injury is not fatal, and besides, a long time has passed. He believes that the death was obviously caused by something else. As a result, both parties abandoned the lawsuit for compensation yesterday and each went to the prosecutor's office to request an autopsy. In the afternoon, Prosecutor Lei, forensic examiner and others crossed the Huangpu River to conduct the examination.

Tragedy of a Broken Anchor Chain

Vegetable Boat Smashed to Pieces

Gu Amao Suffers a Foot Injury

The Yichang steamer, owned by the Taikoo Company of this city, which travels between Yantai and Tianjin, dropped anchor at the Bund outside the Taikoo Wharf to load and unload cargo. Gu Amao's barge, which specializes in transporting vegetables, had unloaded its cargo, and the empty boat was moored under the bow of the Yichang steamer. Gu Amao was sleeping in the cabin, and another crew was sleeping at the stern. Yesterday morning at 7:30, the several-hundred-pound anchor suspended from the bow of the Yichang broke its chain and fell, hitting the barge directly. The boat capsized. The crew sleeping at the stern fell into the Huangpu River and were rescued by another boat. The anchor was very heavy, and the impact of the fall was great, smashing Gu's boat to pieces. Gu's foot was also crushed. The total loss to the boat is estimated to be worth several hundred yuan. He is currently in negotiations with the ship owner to seek compensation.

Youth Struggles for Economic Independence

Attempted Suicide by Overdose of Tranquilizer

Liang Ya-sheng, the third son of Liang Qichao of Guangdong, aged twenty-one, attempted suicide yesterday morning at 11:00 a.m. in a room at the Andong Hotel on Zhengfeng Street by overdosing on tranquilizer. His father's friend, Dr. Wu Liande, discovered him and immediately called a tea boy to escort him to Renji Hospital for treatment. After being injected and given medicine by the doctors, he quickly recovered. According to Liang, after his father's death, he repeatedly sought economic independence, but fate was against him. He felt that life was meaningless and preferred to leave the world early.

Japanese Ship Refuses to Compensate for Collision

The Changping Maru steamer, owned by the Dalian Steamship Company of Japan, collided with a lighter carrying soybean cakes and soybean oil belonging to Liyu Oil Company, a member of the Chinese Grain Exchange, in front of Warehouse No. 6 at the Huangpu Wharf. The cargo was completely submerged, with a loss of 1,495 taels, 9 mace, 3 candareens, and 1 cash. Yesterday, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Japanese Chamber of Commerce, requesting the company to pay the full amount of the loss. After receiving the letter, the Japanese Chamber of Commerce immediately informed the company. The company has replied, stating that the Changping Maru collided with the lighter to avoid danger. The Changping Maru is not responsible for errors caused by acts of necessity, and the company is determined to reject any claims for damages.

Flower Gambling is Truly Harmful

Geese and Ducks Spark a Major Dispute

Mediator Severely Beaten and Injured

In the Dongjiadu area of Tangqiao, Pudong, the practice of flower gambling has become rampant recently. There is even a lottery syndicate located at the Xiaonanmen Wharf at the southern end of Dongjiadu. It dispatches dozens of boatmen every day to solicit gamblers in towns and villages, with hundreds to thousands of cash flowing in and out daily. Three days ago, a Shandong laborer nicknamed "Kuaizi" (chopsticks) at the wharf bet 300 copper coins on "goose" in the syndicate, and the syndicate gave him a slip with the characters "Fengchun" (welcome spring). Kuaizi left without saying anything. When the lottery was drawn, the winning category was "Rongsheng" (flourishing life). After a while, Kuaizi came to claim his winnings, claiming that "Rongsheng" is "goose" as noted in the "Zhifu Quanshu" (Complete Book of Getting Rich, i.e., the flower gambling book). However, the syndicate claimed that "Rongsheng" is "duck" and refused to pay. Kuaizi left angrily. On the afternoon of the day before yesterday, at about 5:00 p.m., he suddenly brought thirty or forty laborers, creating a menacing scene. Kuaizi first grabbed the collar of Zhu, a member of the syndicate, and raised his hand to strike him. The others were also itching for a fight and were about to resort to violence. Shi Jinsheng stepped forward to mediate, but Kuaizi transferred his anger to Shi, using a coal basket rope to lasso Shi's neck. At the same time, he punched and kicked him, severely injuring Shi's head, neck, waist, buttocks, etc. Shi fell to the ground, barely breathing. Seeing that they had caused trouble, the assailants dispersed in a rush. Zhu carried Shi to South Shanghai Hospital for treatment. It is reported that his injuries are critical.

Zhou Wenyong, a five-year-old child, was taken by his older brother to play in front of the Public Sports Ground yesterday morning. Zhou Guitang was riding a bicycle and competing there, causing Wenyong to be knocked down and his abdomen crushed. The child fainted. Xie and the rickshaw overturned, and Xie also injured his hands and feet. The police arrived and took him into custody at the Second District and have handed the case over to the court for investigation.

Insufficient Liquor Tax Stamps Affixed

The Jiangsu Second District White Liquor and Tai Jiabao Tobacco and Liquor Public Sales Tax Collection Office has found that liquor sellers in the Nanshi area often affix insufficient or fake tax stamps on white liquor, or even affix tax stamps loosely to the liquor jars, reusing a single stamp multiple times, engaging in arbitrary fraud, which is detrimental to tax revenue. Therefore, the office has dispatched staff to pay attention to the investigation. The other day, the No. 24 tax inspector of the office, while passing through the Wangjiama Wharf area, found that the Yufengyong Liquor Store, located at No. 101 nearby, had a load of white liquor being sent to Xieqiao by their old manager, Lin Abao, a native of Ningbo, but the tax stamp was only affixed to the jar with one corner. The inspector immediately detained the goods and called the police at that location. Together with the evidence, they were taken to the First Division of the First District. The director ordered them to be detained temporarily, pending a preliminary investigation by the director.

Foreign Potato Boat Sunk by Huge Waves

Qiu Alin, a boatman from the countryside of Pudong, loaded 129 bags of foreign potatoes purchased by cargo owner Zhu Quanlin from the countryside at 6:00 p.m. the night before last and sailed to Shanghai. Because the cargo was too heavy, the boat was hit by huge waves near the Pudong British-American Tobacco Factory, causing it to sink. The potatoes floated away, but the boat was able to resurface. At that time, a small Asiatic Company boat arrived and towed the boat to a nearby beach. It is reported that the loss of goods is about 300 yuan.

Local Court

Detention Center Resumes Visits

The Kangyou Detention Center of the Shanghai Local Court, used for detaining unconvicted criminals, temporarily suspended family visits for a week on the first of this month to reorganize internal affairs and clean up the prisoners. Now that the detention center has been repaired, Chief Prosecutor Liu Maochu has approved the resumption of visits from relatives and friends. As a result, the gate of the detention center has been very crowded in recent days. It is also heard that for the sake of renovating the housing, there will be a large-scale renovation within the month, which will inevitably lead to another suspension of prisoner visits.

The Da Mei Evening News Relocates

The Da Mei Evening News has relocated to the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Rue du Consulat, as the premises on Beijing Road were insufficient. The editorial department is accessed through No. 17, while the circulation and advertising departments are both located at No. 21, right on the corner of Avenue Edward VII and Rue du Consulat.

The Best-Selling Automobile Fuel-Saving Safety Device

Since the Robert Trading Company at No. 39 Sichuan Road began managing the automobile fuel-saving safety device, it has been popular among Chinese and foreign gentlemen and merchants in the city, and demand has greatly exceeded supply. At present, the third batch of stock has little left. A large batch of new goods has been ordered from the United States. It is said that the device can save more than one-quarter of gasoline. The company, for the sake of credibility, also welcomes domestic trials.

Recent News from the Architects' Association

The Chinese Architects' Association was founded in 1926. When it was founded, there were few members, but now it has become the only national architects' association. The number of members is increasing daily. Famous architects from major ports such as Shanghai, Nanjing, Tianjin, Hankou, and Guangzhou have successively joined. The purpose of the association is to connect feelings, research academic studies, help each other in business development, provide architectural services to social welfare, and assist in municipal improvements. Any citizen of the Republic of China who has received specialized architectural education and is engaged in architectural business, or is a professor at an architectural school, may be a member of the association. Anyone who has received secondary education or above and has more than five years of architectural drawing experience may be an associate member of the association. Associate members who have sufficient qualifications may be elected as members. Anyone who agrees with the purpose of the association and has assisted the association may be elected as an honorary member of the association.

Preparatory Committee for the Nanyang National Products Inspection Group

The Shanghai National Products Factory Federation held the first preparatory meeting for the Nanyang Islands Inspection Group yesterday. More than 30 representatives attended. Bian Jiange chaired the meeting. Sun Fuji presented the proposed constitution of the inspection group, which was passed as originally written. Four resolutions were then discussed and passed: (1) The federation will notify all factories that the deadline for registration is the 15th of this month; (2) Factories that are not members of the Shanghai National Products Factory Federation and wish to join in promoting national products must first apply for membership; (3) Each factory is limited to one or two representatives; (4) The next meeting is scheduled to be held on the 18th.

YMCA Harmonica Research Society to Start Classes

The deadline for registration for the YMCA Harmonica Research Society is this Friday evening. Classes will officially start at 7:00 p.m. on the 16th (i.e., next Tuesday). The initial quota was originally limited to 60 people, but it is now almost full. Ladies and gentlemen from all walks of life who are interested in this art are welcome to register with the society as soon as possible to avoid the regret of missing out. In addition, the society has received letters from students of various schools, stating that the teaching time is scheduled for the evening, which is inconvenient for traveling back and forth. They requested a special class. Therefore, an additional class has been added every Wednesday from 5:00 p.m. to 7:00 p.m. to facilitate the participation of the academic community.

Jiuxingtang Establishes a Special National Products Sales Department

Jiuxingtang, located at the Taiping Lane entrance on South Zhonghua Road, Xiaodongmen, has been thriving since its opening. Retail sales of silk scrolls, silver shields, silk fabrics, and printing are the most popular, and it has been overwhelmed with business. Recently, to promote national products, a special national products sales department has been established. Anyone who is interested in doing business but is hampered by economic difficulties can contact the sales department of the store. Sellers do not need capital, and the procedures for selling goods and paying款 are simple. There are no bad habits such as押櫃. The store has printed regulations, which can be obtained at the sales department every day.

News from Various Labor Unions

Rickshaw Pullers' Union: Yesterday afternoon at 4:00, the Second Representative Conference was held at the Xilin Temple on Xilin Road. More than 50 people attended, including He Wushan, Xu Yongxiang, Xu Lin, Huang Guicheng, Han Ganqing, Chen Kunyu, Liu Dehe, Xu Yourong, Shi Fuqing, Bu Yuansheng, etc. Xiao Jinfan chaired the meeting, and Ni Zhiyuan recorded the proceedings. The chairman reported the following: "Our city's rickshaw pullers have repeatedly suffered from local bullies and scoundrels who secretly deploy their gang to steal rickshaws and extort ransoms, depriving them of their possessions and causing unspeakable pain. The rickshaw owners have met Zheng Limin, who, under the guise of providing employment for unemployed workers, falsely reported to the higher authorities and 温放车照, fearing that their business would be affected, and using the workers as tools of resistance. The matter of adding licenses has already been dropped, but the goal of liberation has not yet been achieved. The rickshaw owners, taking advantage of the lack of leadership, suddenly want to increase rickshaw rent, making it difficult for the workers to make a living from their hard work. Moreover, they are faced with high prices for rice and firewood. Under such oppressive circumstances, how can their suffering be permanently eradicated? The launch of this association is truly a way to seek our own liberation." The discussions included: (1) Submitting a request to the higher authorities for registration; (2) Drafting the detailed regulations of the association; (3) Dividing the association into six district associations; (4) Sending a letter to thank the Municipal Public Security Bureau and the Detective Team for protecting the workers of the association and strictly cracking down on rickshaw thieves; (5) Hiring Xiao Jinfan as an instructor and Deng Bosen as a secretary; (6) Determining the date and location of the preparatory committee election; (7) The preparatory committee will notify the rickshaw workers.

A two-day advertisement will be placed in various newspapers. All resolutions were passed unanimously, and the meeting was adjourned.

Letter

To the Editor:

Regarding the item "Collision between Warship and Merchant Ship" in the local news section of your newspaper on September 7th, the name of the warship was said to be the Chinese Navy's Weisheng warship, which seems to be a mistake. Upon checking, our ship was stationed at Huangshi Port two months ago and was damaged by the Japanese ship Dalimaru. Last month, it was being repaired at the Jiangnan Shipyard of the Navy and is still berthed at the Gaochangmiao Wharf and has not yet been completed. The so-called collision with the Yunnan steamer did not happen to our ship. I am sending this letter so that you may make corrections.

Sincerely,

Weisheng Warship

September 7, 1927
