Youth Garden

Night Trip to Wusong

— Su Duyu

Ling, Qiong, Yinlin, Hezi, and myself, a total of five people, were all happy and agreed to go to Wusong for fun. When it comes to having fun, who wouldn't be happy? So, it was decided to go to the seaside on the 14th.

As agreed, the four of us would gather at Ling's house at 7 PM. That day, I had dinner—no, just a snack—at 6:30 PM and went to Ling's house on North Sichuan Road, which was filled with Cantonese flavors.

She looked at the clock, it was only 6:45, and she said to me in surprise,

(Your watch must be fast.)

I didn't understand what she meant. After she explained, I realized she was saying why I was so punctual because she expected us to arrive at least by 7:30 PM. I wanted to say something then, but a small voice in my heart seemed to say, (Are you going to start with your usual clichés again?) So I retracted my long speech and changed it to a playful remark,

(Wouldn't coming earlier shorten the time?)

She was confused by my words, looking at me with a puzzled expression, her eyes wide open, deeply giving off a question mark...

I smiled silently, looked at her, and said,

(I feel like the clock at your house runs much faster.)

She smiled lightly, seeming to say, (Then why don't you make your clock run faster?) Finally, she said that to me. We laughed heartily. In fact, wouldn't anyone who isn't an idiot or a dumb ox understand what I meant? I expected that she would understand.

The clock struck seven. Soon after, thankfully, everyone was punctual. Qiong, Hezi, and Yinlin arrived at the same time. When asked why they came together, they said that Hezi had gone to each of their homes to gather them.

Once everyone was together, we naturally started walking. Yinlin and I carried the snacks, Hezi took the soda, and Ling and Qiong jointly carried a leather bag for cups and other things. Each of us had a task, so we took the public bus to the Tiantong'an Station. Because there is now a small train that runs 77 times a day, there is a train every fifteen minutes. Looking at the train schedule, the next train to Wusong was only two minutes away. We hurried to buy tickets. Although we say "hurried," we still pushed and shoved each other as if there was some benefit to抢着. In fact, this kind of politeness is unnecessary, it would be more straightforward for each person to buy their own ticket. However, at that time, ideal couldn't overcome the environment, and I also挤 to buy a ticket. This really surprised me—in the end, Hezi bought tickets for all of us.

When the train came, we used "squeeze" again. Fortunately, we didn't get separated, and the five of us boarded the same carriage. Soon after, the train started. A bit of wind came into the stuffy carriage. Although the wind was mixed with a lot of coal smoke, it was much better than being闷着.

The train swayed forward. In less than five minutes, we were in Jiangwan. The four square characters of Lida Academy, accompanied by a red heart—the school emblem of Lida—were clearly visible. But the train passed quickly, and I couldn't see many of my school friends in Lida. I don't know what they are doing now. I can only say sorry here—I can't travel with you. Especially my friend Mr. Wu, and the two ladies, Ms. Zhu and Ms. Wen.

After Lida is Jiangwan Station. After a pause, the large clock standing at Labor University? was clearly visible. Looking left from the large clock, there is Lida facing it. Between these two schools, there are some houses. In some houses, my school friend Ms. Cheng lives and watches. I can only look over there with a "helpless" look. In the end, I couldn't join her for a trip.

The train started again, sounded a whistle, and finally pulled my sight back to the car. Ling? Still talking happily. Although Cheng Zhu? and the others didn't come, Ling is here. She looks so much like Cheng. Like Cheng, she also divides her short hair into two forks in the back, fully expressing a naive girl. Also, Qiong's eloquence is not much different from Zhu's. As for Yinlin and Hezi, they also love to joke around. With them, how can we be lonely?

The jumbled conversation continued non-stop. The train stopped at Wusong Station. One by one, we all happily carried our belongings and jumped off the train. The five of us talked and laughed as we walked to the river.

A bright moon burned with clear white light, sprinkling it on everything on the ground. The sea gently rippled, and the moon's light was reflected in the convex and concave water waves, like flickering eyes, like scales, star-like shining. The calm sea was carved with infinite beauty. Looking up at the sky, except for a few larger constellations that could still be seen, most of the unknown thousands of small stars seemed to be hidden as if they were forced by the bright moon. I couldn't help but tell everyone this idea. Qiong playfully pointed to the sea surface. The moonlit waves showed a little bit of light like stars. ? Didn't speak, just laughed. Finally, he forcefully stopped laughing and said,

(Duyu, they are here.)

I admire her eloquence. I hope that such stubborn stars will鑽进enter her chest, illuminating her entire belly with light. At the same time, I will not fail her instructed grandness and answer her by saying,

(Oh, they are really stubborn. Although they can't beat the moon's power, then, then they will go to another place to create their world.)

(But, Duyu, they are hypocritical. Are you willing to pay attention to this point of theirs?) Ling said to me. I couldn't help but sink into thought because of this sentence.

(But such beautiful water waves, can I bear to say that they are伪 fake stars?) I said.

Besides the sound of the sea gently hitting the shore, making small water sounds, there was only the sound of our leather shoes, and Ling and my conversation. She seemed to scoop out her heart, talking very enthusiastically about such things. The ten eyes of the five people patrolled the boundless ocean. From time to time, a few ships emerged with black smoke, becoming a thin line, appearing and disappearing remotely where the water and sky meet. So I would say,

(How magnificent this atmosphere is.)

Hezi, who has always advocated that proletarian literature has the necessity of existing, objected, (But do you know the suffering of the stokers and mechanics who are driving the ships? We are now leisurely enjoying this night trip here, while they are suffering.)

He considers himself a lover of proletarian literature. I used to praise proletarian literature in the same way as him, but recently the rapid tide of the national literature movement touched my heart. I objectively recognized the hypocrisy of proletarian literature. I have long decided to stay away from it. After making such a decision, I once publicized the characteristics and mission of national literature in detail among my friends. Although a little effect has been achieved, like Hezi, he will sometimes admit the benefits of national literature, but suddenly he will go to赞成 support proletarianism again. Tonight he is singing the old tune again, so I can't help but start my theory and say to him,

(Hezi, you should understand the hypocrisy of proletarian literature and not be driven by it. Class war is extremely畸形 deformed. In Soviet Russia, there may be his environment that makes it so, but in China, the environment昭示 revealed to us that it is not the harm of class that has made China so poor and weak. It is really the rampage and oppression of imperialists that has made the Chinese nation turn to污泥 mud. The suffering of the stokers and others in the ship that you are talking about now, we should sympathize with this suffering. If he is working for Chinese merchant ships, although he has suffered hardship, this is his national duty, and he should contribute to the country's transportation business. When we talk about the nation now, we should no longer just self-deceive ourselves with (spiritual civilization), but also start to catch up with the material civilization of the East and the West. This transportation business is a kind of material civilization. It can do a basic job for material civilization. This kind of work is meaningful and upward. We have to praise them and encourage them. What do you think is right? As for the problem of their living expenses, I think it should naturally be a little more generous, because only under a satisfying life can we create better achievements for society.)

He seemed to obey again, responding with (Yes, yes.)

Smoke billows from the ship's chimney, appearing and disappearing where the water and sky meet. Remotely, the five of us silently walked quietly.

Time passed in talk and laughter. The things we brought were all packed in everyone's belly. The bright moon has also risen high, hanging near the top of our heads. Everyone suggested going back. Unanimously approved, we took light steps, hanging a心 heart that had been fully excited, and walked into the train.

The car carried us back to Tiantong'an Station. A few people in the lonely car raised their steps and each踏着 walked on the silent road back to their destination to安宿 settle.

A Proposal

The ruthless韶光 time, like flowing water, has passed away. In the blink of an eye, it is another high autumn and refreshing weather. People who have generally suffered under the赤帝 red emperor's power feel a little cool. At this time, various schools are busy preparing for the start of school. A group of students who have放浪 indulged for a summer vacation have to蹩顿 curb themselves and pick up their schoolbags and go to school again. But before entering the school, a problem arises. What is the problem? It seems that these words are written on the two school gates (No money, no entry). Of course, you have to pay tuition fees before entering school. This tuition fee problem does not cause any difficulties for the children of rich families, but what about the children of poor families? During this period of米珠薪桂 rice as pearls and cinnamon as firewood, fathers and brothers use sweat and blood money to spend on a family that cannot even eat enough to be warm. Where can they have spare money for their children to go to school? For the sake of this万恶 evil money, I don't know how many ambitious young people have been buried. For the sake of grief and anger, they take the path of消极 negativity—many of them are堕落 fallen. How sad and painful this is for us.

In my personal feeling, the strength or weakness of a country is closely related to education. Our country has declined to such a point because education is not普及 popular—the people lack knowledge. If we want the country to be strong, we must普及 popularize education. If we want to普及 popularize education, we must solve the above难題 problem. But how can we solve it? Schools have all kinds of expenses and of course they cannot let us study for free. The only way is for the government to set up a few work-study schools to cultivate this class of ambitious people who want to study but have no ability. If we do this, I believe education can普及 popularize and our country can become strong. (Peizhen)

Social News

Interview with George Bernard Shaw (1)

— Lin

— A Lovable Child of Seventy-Three —

Swells Stokes published an article about George Bernard Shaw in (The New Statesman), saying, "The most exciting thing in my life has been the time I recently spent alone with George Bernard Shaw. I have never met, nor do I expect to meet again, a more lovable child of seventy-three. If any woman can be forgiven for jealousy, it is Mrs. Shaw, because her husband's lovableness makes everyone he meets praise him. His youth is completely迷感 fascinating. He is so young, thin, and joyful that one suspects he has made some secret pact with the devil, like Faust. To put it plainly, he is a young man who will keep his youth until death. If physical health is of great value, then his death will probably not happen while I am alive. I think there are still fifty years of work to be done."

The legend says that a drowning person sees his entire past in a moment before he dies, but if George Bernard Shaw were ever to reach this point—Heaven forbid—what he would see would not be the past but the future. His inclination is different from that of people of his age. He has great interest in the future and attaches great importance to progress. He pays great attention to new creations. I asked him, (Are you interested in sound movies?)

This was a stupid question, but I often hear senior gentlemen criticize sound movies, and the old gentlemen are very enthusiastic about this little condemnation. In this way, before I thought that the person I was talking to was a enthusiastic youth, this question had already slipped out of my mouth.

(I am very interested in sound movies,) George Bernard Shaw replied, (I will tell you why.) He really told me that he was very interested in this new creation of movies because with this medium, he could finally make his perfect drama public to the world.

(This is impossible,) he said, (To obtain a perfect drama production on stage, for example, a drama director practices the script very carefully, and it looks almost perfect on Monday night, but who dares to say what it will become on Tuesday? After that, a伶人 actor can复演 replay a script without any change. It looks very good on the first night, but it regresses on the second night, but the film has one advantage. Capturing drama through film can achieve a perfect production. Like Chaplin, it can take a lot of time to make a film ten金 ten美 perfect, and finally he will connect the fragments. The result is a perfect product that is传之 permanent.)

(Then why didn't you agree to have your dramas made into films before?) I asked George Bernard Shaw, knowing the answer to this question. But I wanted him to tell me personally.

He said, (Before the invention of sound movies, film merchants did not want my dramas, and the same was true for others. I knew they would buy scripts, but why? Dramas are made up of dialogue. When making films, the dialogue is completely removed, so a successful film drama is not a drama at all.)

Often Thorough

George Bernard Shaw is often thorough. I remember Sir Philip Gibbs telling me how surprised he was when he took this playwright to the aircraft camp during the war and heard him tell people about the many knowledge of their machines, like a skilled mechanic. The same is true for sound movies. George Bernard Shaw carefully studied this matter as if it were his lifelong career. He had very little unclear about the reproduction of sound. In recent years, he has been very interested in studying phonographs and other methods of storing sound.

He said to me, (The difficulty is that individuals are呌 called inexperienced beauty dramatists to move or speak. He never tells伊 them the speed of the most important movements and speeches. Several years ago, a filmmaker asked me to take a segment of film. They told me that康拉 and仁惠尔 had already been tested, so I agreed to this request. When the卡麥拉 camera was taking my movements, I walked into a room, took off my hat, sat down, and took a pen in my hand to start my work. I did these movements very naturally as usual, but when I saw it reflected on the screen, it became like this,)

During our conversation, George Bernard Shaw rose from the couch and mimicked the action shown on the screen for me. This proved that he was as talented a伶人 actor as his dramatic genius. Every one of his gestures was strangely funny and made people laugh, as if it were taken with a slow-motion camera.

He sat down again and said, (They should tell me to restrain my natural movements. You understand that a person does not have to move for the film, just move gently. Even if a person's thoughts can be translated into movements for the camera, an伶人 actor only wants to move an impression onto the screen.) George Bernard Shaw went on to say solemnly, (I don't mean that most movie stars can think for themselves, but a producer can tell them what to think.)

Returning to the issue of sound reproduction, George Bernard Shaw said, (The success of that matter also depends on the speed at which the record rotates during production. When it rotates slowly, the collected sound is accurate and easy to distinguish. In fact, a phonograph record just calls people to reveal their original appearance. A record that调和 harmonizes its appropriate speed can clearly indicate the origin of this person. At my home in the countryside, there is a record that was recorded before. If that record is slowly started, you can hear me speaking in exquisite Irish pronunciation. I sing the old丐 beggar on杜白林 Dublin street. If the speed increases, my voice gradually合乎 conforms to the rule, ending with you hearing me speak as I do now.)

Shanghai-Japan Facsimile Plan

The Japanese side will propose it during telegram negotiations

The World News Agency says, according to Japanese news, the revised negotiations on the Sino-Japanese submarine telegraph will be officially started in Shanghai by Minister Wang Chongguang, acting as ambassador, and Sino-Japanese expert commissioners.
